## üîß 1. Complete Pixel Art Generator (`generators/pixel_art_generator.py`)

```python
# generators/pixel_art_generator.py
import numpy as np
from PIL import Image, ImageDraw, ImageFont, ImageColor
import json
import os
import math

class PixelArtGenerator:
    def __init__(self, output_dir="dvr-assets"):
        self.output_dir = output_dir
        self.colors = {
            'gold': '#FFD700',
            'cyber_green': '#00FF88', 
            'crimson': '#FF4500',
            'purple': '#8A2BE2',
            'dark_bg': '#0A0A19',
            'light_accent': '#1A1A3E',
            'white': '#FFFFFF',
            'black': '#000000',
            'silver': '#C0C0C0',
            'blue': '#0080FF',
            'orange': '#FF8000',
            'red': '#FF0000',
            'dark_gray': '#404040',
            'light_gray': '#808080'
        }
        self.setup_directories()

    def setup_directories(self):
        """Create all necessary directories"""
        dirs = [
            f"{self.output_dir}/icons/16x16/status",
            f"{self.output_dir}/icons/16x16/actions", 
            f"{self.output_dir}/icons/16x16/emotions",
            f"{self.output_dir}/icons/16x16/blockchain",
            f"{self.output_dir}/icons/16x16/weapons",
            f"{self.output_dir}/icons/16x16/vehicles",
            f"{self.output_dir}/icons/32x32/characters",
            f"{self.output_dir}/icons/32x32/buildings",
            f"{self.output_dir}/icons/32x32/resources",
            f"{self.output_dir}/sprites/animated",
            f"{self.output_dir}/sprites/static/ui-elements",
            f"{self.output_dir}/sprites/static/backgrounds"
        ]
        for dir_path in dirs:
            os.makedirs(dir_path, exist_ok=True)
        print(f"‚úÖ Created directory structure in {self.output_dir}")

    def create_status_icon(self, name, color, pattern):
        """Generate 16x16 status icons with various patterns"""
        img = Image.new('RGBA', (16, 16), (0, 0, 0, 0))
        draw = ImageDraw.Draw(img)
        
        if pattern == 'success':
            # Checkmark
            draw.line([(4, 8), (7, 11), (12, 6)], fill=color, width=2)
            draw.ellipse([2, 2, 14, 14], outline=color, width=1)
            
        elif pattern == 'error':
            # X with circle
            draw.line([(4, 4), (12, 12)], fill=color, width=2)
            draw.line([(4, 12), (12, 4)], fill=color, width=2)
            draw.ellipse([2, 2, 14, 14], outline=color, width=1)
            
        elif pattern == 'warning':
            # Exclamation in triangle
            draw.polygon([(8, 2), (3, 13), (13, 13)], outline=color, width=1)
            draw.line([(8, 5), (8, 9)], fill=color, width=2)
            draw.ellipse([7, 11, 9, 13], fill=color)
            
        elif pattern == 'thinking':
            # Brain with pulsing dots
            draw.ellipse([4, 4, 12, 12], outline=color, width=1)
            draw.arc([5, 5, 11, 11], 0, 180, fill=color, width=1)
            draw.arc([6, 6, 10, 10], 180, 360, fill=color, width=1)
            # Dots around
            for angle in range(0, 360, 45):
                x = 8 + int(6 * math.cos(math.radians(angle)))
                y = 8 + int(6 * math.sin(math.radians(angle)))
                draw.ellipse([x-1, y-1, x+1, y+1], fill=color)
                
        elif pattern == 'sync':
            # Circular arrows
            draw.arc([3, 3, 13, 13], 45, 225, fill=color, width=2)
            draw.arc([3, 3, 13, 13], 225, 405, fill=color, width=2)
            # Arrow heads
            draw.polygon([(11, 5), (13, 3), (11, 1)], fill=color)
            draw.polygon([(5, 11), (3, 13), (1, 11)], fill=color)
        
        img.save(f"{self.output_dir}/icons/16x16/status/{name}.png")
        print(f"‚úÖ Created status icon: {name}")
        return img

    def create_action_icon(self, name, icon_type):
        """Generate 16x16 action icons with detailed pixel art"""
        img = Image.new('RGBA', (16, 16), (0, 0, 0, 0))
        draw = ImageDraw.Draw(img)
        
        if icon_type == 'solar':
            # Solar panel with detailed rays
            draw.rectangle([4, 7, 12, 11], fill=self.colors['gold'], 
                         outline=self.colors['white'], width=1)
            # Grid pattern on panel
            draw.line([(6, 7), (6, 11)], fill=self.colors['white'])
            draw.line([(8, 7), (8, 11)], fill=self.colors['white'])
            draw.line([(10, 7), (10, 11)], fill=self.colors['white'])
            # Sun rays
            for i in range(3, 14, 2):
                draw.line([(i, 4), (i, 6)], fill=self.colors['gold'], width=1)
            # Support stand
            draw.line([(8, 11), (8, 13)], fill=self.colors['dark_gray'], width=2)
                
        elif icon_type == 'trade':
            # Detailed coin with gear overlay
            draw.ellipse([3, 3, 13, 13], fill=self.colors['gold'], 
                        outline=self.colors['white'], width=1)
            # Coin details
            draw.ellipse([5, 5, 11, 11], outline=self.colors['white'], width=1)
            draw.text((7, 6), "$", fill=self.colors['white'])
            # Gear overlay
            draw.polygon([(8, 1), (9, 3), (11, 2), (13, 4), (11, 6), (9, 5), 
                         (8, 7), (7, 5), (5, 6), (3, 4), (5, 2), (7, 3)], 
                        outline=self.colors['silver'], width=1)
            
        elif icon_type == 'energy':
            # Detailed lightning bolt
            draw.polygon([(5, 1), (8, 1), (6, 7), (9, 7), (7, 15), (4, 15), 
                         (6, 9), (3, 9)], fill=self.colors['cyber_green'])
            # Electric aura
            draw.polygon([(4, 0), (9, 0), (7, 8), (10, 8), (8, 16), (3, 16), 
                         (5, 8), (2, 8)], outline=self.colors['white'], width=1)
                         
        elif icon_type == 'water':
            # Water drop with waves
            draw.ellipse([6, 2, 10, 8], fill=self.colors['blue'])
            draw.polygon([(8, 2), (6, 8), (10, 8)], fill=self.colors['blue'])
            # Waves at bottom
            for y in range(10, 15, 2):
                for x in range(2, 14, 4):
                    draw.arc([x, y, x+2, y+2], 0, 180, fill=self.colors['blue'], width=1)
            
        elif icon_type == 'food':
            # Apple or food item
            draw.ellipse([4, 6, 12, 14], fill=self.colors['red'])
            draw.ellipse([6, 4, 8, 8], fill=self.colors['cyber_green'])  # Leaf
            draw.line([(7, 2), (7, 6)], fill=self.colors['dark_gray'], width=1)  # Stem
            
        img.save(f"{self.output_dir}/icons/16x16/actions/{name}.png")
        print(f"‚úÖ Created action icon: {name}")
        return img

    def create_blockchain_icon(self, name, blockchain_type):
        """Generate 16x16 blockchain-specific icons"""
        img = Image.new('RGBA', (16, 16), (0, 0, 0, 0))
        draw = ImageDraw.Draw(img)
        
        if blockchain_type == 'bitcoin':
            # Bitcoin symbol
            draw.ellipse([2, 2, 14, 14], fill=self.colors['gold'], 
                        outline=self.colors['white'], width=1)
            # B symbol (simplified)
            draw.rectangle([5, 5, 6, 11], fill=self.colors['white'])
            draw.rectangle([6, 5, 10, 7], fill=self.colors['white'])
            draw.rectangle([6, 8, 9, 9], fill=self.colors['white'])
            draw.rectangle([6, 10, 10, 11], fill=self.colors['white'])
            
        elif blockchain_type == 'ethereum':
            # Ethereum diamond
            draw.polygon([(8, 2), (12, 8), (8, 10), (4, 8)], 
                        fill=self.colors['blue'], outline=self.colors['white'])
            draw.polygon([(8, 2), (10, 6), (8, 7), (6, 6)], 
                        fill=self.colors['light_gray'])
            draw.polygon([(8, 7), (12, 8), (8, 14), (4, 8)], 
                        fill=self.colors['dark_gray'])
                        
        elif blockchain_type == 'nft':
            # NFT card with image placeholder
            draw.rectangle([3, 3, 13, 13], fill=self.colors['purple'], 
                         outline=self.colors['white'], width=1)
            draw.rectangle([4, 4, 12, 9], fill=self.colors['dark_bg'])
            draw.rectangle([4, 10, 12, 12], fill=self.colors['light_accent'])
            # Image placeholder
            draw.line([(5, 5), (11, 8)], fill=self.colors['white'], width=1)
            draw.line([(5, 8), (11, 5)], fill=self.colors['white'], width=1)
            
        elif blockchain_type == 'token':
            # Generic token
            draw.ellipse([3, 3, 13, 13], fill=self.colors['cyber_green'], 
                        outline=self.colors['white'], width=1)
            draw.ellipse([5, 5, 11, 11], outline=self.colors['white'], width=1)
            draw.text((7, 6), "T", fill=self.colors['white'])
            
        elif blockchain_type == 'smart_contract':
            # Contract/document with chain link
            draw.rectangle([4, 2, 11, 12], fill=self.colors['white'], 
                         outline=self.colors['black'], width=1)
            draw.line([(5, 4), (10, 4)], fill=self.colors['black'])
            draw.line([(5, 6), (10, 6)], fill=self.colors['black'])
            draw.line([(5, 8), (8, 8)], fill=self.colors['black'])
            # Chain link
            draw.ellipse([1, 10, 5, 14], outline=self.colors['gold'], width=1)
            draw.ellipse([3, 12, 7, 16], outline=self.colors['gold'], width=1)
            
        elif blockchain_type == 'wallet':
            # Digital wallet
            draw.rectangle([3, 5, 13, 12], fill=self.colors['dark_gray'], 
                         outline=self.colors['white'], width=1)
            draw.rectangle([4, 6, 12, 11], fill=self.colors['black'])
            # Cards inside
            draw.rectangle([5, 7, 11, 8], fill=self.colors['gold'])
            draw.rectangle([5, 9, 11, 10], fill=self.colors['silver'])
            # Lock
            draw.rectangle([7, 2, 9, 5], outline=self.colors['white'], width=1)
            draw.ellipse([7, 1, 9, 4], outline=self.colors['white'], width=1)
            
        img.save(f"{self.output_dir}/icons/16x16/blockchain/{name}.png")
        print(f"‚úÖ Created blockchain icon: {name}")
        return img

    def create_weapon_icon(self, name, weapon_type):
        """Generate 16x16 weapon icons"""
        img = Image.new('RGBA', (16, 16), (0, 0, 0, 0))
        draw = ImageDraw.Draw(img)
        
        if weapon_type == 'rifle':
            # Assault rifle
            draw.rectangle([2, 7, 14, 9], fill=self.colors['dark_gray'])  # Barrel
            draw.rectangle([8, 6, 12, 10], fill=self.colors['black'])     # Body
            draw.rectangle([11, 5, 13, 11], fill=self.colors['dark_gray']) # Stock
            draw.rectangle([6, 8, 8, 10], fill=self.colors['dark_gray'])  # Trigger guard
            draw.rectangle([4, 6, 6, 7], fill=self.colors['black'])       # Sight
            
        elif weapon_type == 'pistol':
            # Handgun
            draw.rectangle([4, 7, 10, 9], fill=self.colors['dark_gray'])  # Barrel
            draw.rectangle([8, 6, 12, 10], fill=self.colors['black'])     # Grip
            draw.rectangle([6, 8, 8, 10], fill=self.colors['dark_gray'])  # Trigger
            draw.rectangle([3, 6, 5, 7], fill=self.colors['black'])       # Sight
            
        elif weapon_type == 'sword':
            # Medieval sword
            draw.rectangle([7, 2, 9, 12], fill=self.colors['silver'])     # Blade
            draw.rectangle([6, 10, 10, 12], fill=self.colors['gold'])     # Guard
            draw.rectangle([7, 12, 9, 14], fill=self.colors['dark_gray']) # Handle
            draw.ellipse([7, 1, 9, 3], fill=self.colors['silver'])        # Tip
            
        elif weapon_type == 'bow':
            # Bow and arrow
            draw.arc([4, 2, 12, 14], 270, 450, fill=self.colors['dark_gray'], width=2)
            draw.line([(6, 3), (6, 13)], fill=self.colors['white'])       # String
            draw.line([(2, 8), (8, 8)], fill=self.colors['gold'], width=1) # Arrow
            draw.polygon([(1, 7), (1, 9), (3, 8)], fill=self.colors['silver']) # Arrow head
            
        elif weapon_type == 'grenade':
            # Hand grenade
            draw.ellipse([5, 6, 11, 12], fill=self.colors['dark_gray'])
            draw.rectangle([7, 4, 9, 6], fill=self.colors['black'])       # Pin area
            draw.line([(8, 2), (8, 4)], fill=self.colors['silver'], width=2) # Pin
            # Texture lines
            draw.line([(6, 8), (10, 8)], fill=self.colors['black'])
            draw.line([(6, 10), (10, 10)], fill=self.colors['black'])
            
        elif weapon_type == 'sniper':
            # Sniper rifle with scope
            draw.rectangle([2, 7, 14, 9], fill=self.colors['dark_gray'])  # Barrel
            draw.rectangle([8, 6, 12, 10], fill=self.colors['black'])     # Body
            draw.ellipse([5, 5, 9, 9], outline=self.colors['black'], width=1) # Scope
            draw.ellipse([6, 6, 8, 8], fill=self.colors['red'])          # Scope lens
            draw.rectangle([11, 5, 13, 11], fill=self.colors['dark_gray']) # Stock
            
        img.save(f"{self.output_dir}/icons/16x16/weapons/{name}.png")
        print(f"‚úÖ Created weapon icon: {name}")
        return img

    def create_vehicle_icon(self, name, vehicle_type):
        """Generate 16x16 vehicle icons"""
        img = Image.new('RGBA', (16, 16), (0, 0, 0, 0))
        draw = ImageDraw.Draw(img)
        
        if vehicle_type == 'car':
            # Standard car
            draw.rectangle([3, 8, 13, 12], fill=self.colors['blue'])      # Body
            draw.rectangle([5, 6, 11, 8], fill=self.colors['light_gray']) # Windshield
            draw.ellipse([2, 10, 6, 14], fill=self.colors['black'])       # Left wheel
            draw.ellipse([10, 10, 14, 14], fill=self.colors['black'])     # Right wheel
            draw.ellipse([3, 11, 5, 13], fill=self.colors['dark_gray'])   # Left rim
            draw.ellipse([11, 11, 13, 13], fill=self.colors['dark_gray']) # Right rim
            
        elif vehicle_type == 'truck':
            # Pickup truck
            draw.rectangle([2, 8, 14, 12], fill=self.colors['red'])       # Body
            draw.rectangle([2, 6, 8, 8], fill=self.colors['light_gray'])  # Cab
            draw.rectangle([9, 8, 13, 10], fill=self.colors['dark_gray']) # Bed
            draw.ellipse([1, 10, 5, 14], fill=self.colors['black'])       # Left wheel
            draw.ellipse([11, 10, 15, 14], fill=self.colors['black'])     # Right wheel
            
        elif vehicle_type == 'motorcycle':
            # Motorcycle
            draw.ellipse([2, 8, 6, 12], fill=self.colors['black'])        # Front wheel
            draw.ellipse([10, 8, 14, 12], fill=self.colors['black'])      # Rear wheel
            draw.line([(4, 10), (8, 6)], fill=self.colors['silver'], width=2) # Front fork
            draw.line([(8, 6), (12, 10)], fill=self.colors['silver'], width=2) # Frame
            draw.rectangle([7, 5, 9, 7], fill=self.colors['red'])         # Tank
            draw.line([(6, 4), (10, 4)], fill=self.colors['black'], width=2) # Handlebars
            
        elif vehicle_type == 'helicopter':
            # Helicopter
            draw.ellipse([4, 8, 12, 12], fill=self.colors['dark_gray'])   # Body
            draw.rectangle([6, 6, 10, 8], fill=self.colors['light_gray']) # Cockpit
            draw.line([(1, 2), (15, 2)], fill=self.colors['dark_gray'], width=2) # Main rotor
            draw.line([(8, 1), (8, 6)], fill=self.colors['black'], width=1) # Rotor shaft
            draw.line([(12, 8), (14, 6)], fill=self.colors['black'], width=1) # Tail
            draw.line([(14, 5), (14, 7)], fill=self.colors['dark_gray'], width=2) # Tail rotor
            
        elif vehicle_type == 'tank':
            # Military tank
            draw.rectangle([2, 8, 14, 12], fill=self.colors['dark_gray']) # Hull
            draw.rectangle([4, 6, 12, 8], fill=self.colors['dark_gray'])  # Turret
            draw.rectangle([6, 4, 14, 6], fill=self.colors['black'])      # Barrel
            # Track details
            for x in range(3, 13, 2):
                draw.rectangle([x, 10, x+1, 11], fill=self.colors['black'])
            draw.ellipse([2, 9, 4, 11], fill=self.colors['black'])        # Drive wheel
            draw.ellipse([12, 9, 14, 11], fill=self.colors['black'])      # Drive wheel
            
        elif vehicle_type == 'boat':
            # Boat
            draw.polygon([(3, 12), (13, 12), (12, 10), (4, 10)], fill=self.colors['white']) # Hull
            draw.rectangle([7, 8, 9, 10], fill=self.colors['dark_gray'])  # Mast
            draw.polygon([(9, 4), (9, 8), (13, 6)], fill=self.colors['white']) # Sail
            draw.line([(2, 13), (14, 13)], fill=self.colors['blue'], width=2) # Water line
            
        img.save(f"{self.output_dir}/icons/16x16/vehicles/{name}.png")
        print(f"‚úÖ Created vehicle icon: {name}")
        return img

    def create_npc_character(self, name, character_type):
        """Generate 32x32 NPC character sprites"""
        img = Image.new('RGBA', (32, 32), (0, 0, 0, 0))
        draw = ImageDraw.Draw(img)
        
        # Base character silhouette
        draw.ellipse([12, 4, 20, 12], fill=self.colors['light_gray'])     # Head
        draw.rectangle([14, 12, 18, 24], fill=self.colors['white'])       # Body
        draw.rectangle([12, 20, 14, 28], fill=self.colors['blue'])        # Left leg
        draw.rectangle([18, 20, 20, 28], fill=self.colors['blue'])        # Right leg
        draw.rectangle([10, 14, 12, 20], fill=self.colors['light_gray'])  # Left arm
        draw.rectangle([20, 14, 22, 20], fill=self.colors['light_gray'])  # Right arm
        
        # Character-specific features
        if character_type == 'trader':
            draw.rectangle([12, 16, 20, 20], fill=self.colors['gold'])    # Gold vest
            draw.ellipse([8, 18, 12, 22], fill=self.colors['gold'])       # Coin bag
            draw.ellipse([7, 6, 9, 8], fill=self.colors['black'])         # Left eye
            draw.ellipse([11, 6, 13, 8], fill=self.colors['black'])       # Right eye
            draw.arc([8, 8, 12, 10], 0, 180, fill=self.colors['black'])   # Smile
            
        elif character_type == 'engineer':
            draw.rectangle([13, 14, 19, 16], fill=self.colors['cyber_green'])  # Tool belt
            draw.rectangle([6, 12, 10, 14], fill=self.colors['dark_gray'])     # Wrench
            draw.rectangle([22, 12, 26, 14], fill=self.colors['silver'])       # Screwdriver
            draw.rectangle([14, 10, 18, 12], fill=self.colors['red'])          # Hard hat
            draw.ellipse([7, 6, 9, 8], fill=self.colors['black'])              # Left eye
            draw.ellipse([11, 6, 13, 8], fill=self.colors['black'])            # Right eye
            
        elif character_type == 'warrior':
            draw.rectangle([12, 16, 20, 20], fill=self.colors['dark_gray'])    # Armor
            draw.rectangle([6, 14, 10, 18], fill=self.colors['silver'])        # Shield
            draw.rectangle([22, 10, 26, 20], fill=self.colors['silver'])       # Sword
            draw.rectangle([14, 10, 18, 12], fill=self.colors['dark_gray'])    # Helmet
            draw.ellipse([7, 6, 9, 8], fill=self.colors['red'])                # Left eye (glowing)
            draw.ellipse([11, 6, 13, 8], fill=self.colors['red'])              # Right eye (glowing)
            
        elif character_type == 'mage':
            draw.rectangle([12, 16, 20, 24], fill=self.colors['purple'])       # Robe
            draw.rectangle([22, 8, 26, 16], fill=self.colors['gold'])          # Staff
            draw.ellipse([24, 6, 26, 8], fill=self.colors['blue'])             # Magic orb
            draw.polygon([(16, 4), (14, 8), (18, 8)], fill=self.colors['purple']) # Wizard hat
            draw.ellipse([7, 6, 9, 8], fill=self.colors['blue'])               # Left eye (magical)
            draw.ellipse([11, 6, 13, 8], fill=self.colors['blue'])             # Right eye (magical)
            
        img.save(f"{self.output_dir}/icons/32x32/characters/{name}.png")
        print(f"‚úÖ Created character: {name}")
        return img

    def create_building_icon(self, name, building_type):
        """Generate 32x32 building icons"""
        img = Image.new('RGBA', (32, 32), (0, 0, 0, 0))
        draw = ImageDraw.Draw(img)
        
        if building_type == 'solar_farm':
            # Solar panel array
            for row in range(2):
                for col in range(3):
                    x = 4 + col * 8
                    y = 16 + row * 6
                    draw.rectangle([x, y, x+6, y+4], fill=self.colors['blue'], 
                                 outline=self.colors['white'], width=1)
                    # Panel lines
                    draw.line([(x+2, y), (x+2, y+4)], fill=self.colors['white'])
                    draw.line([(x+4, y), (x+4, y+4)], fill=self.colors['white'])
            
            # Support structure
            draw.line([(16, 22), (16, 28)], fill=self.colors['dark_gray'], width=2)
            
        elif building_type == 'trading_post':
            # Building structure
            draw.rectangle([8, 12, 24, 28], fill=self.colors['dark_gray'], 
                         outline=self.colors['white'], width=1)
            # Roof
            draw.polygon([(6, 12), (16, 4), (26, 12)], fill=self.colors['red'])
            # Door
            draw.rectangle([14, 20, 18, 28], fill=self.colors['black'])
            # Windows
            draw.rectangle([10, 16, 12, 18], fill=self.colors['gold'])
            draw.rectangle([20, 16, 22, 18], fill=self.colors['gold'])
            # Sign
            draw.rectangle([12, 8, 20, 12], fill=self.colors['gold'])
            
        elif building_type == 'fortress':
            # Main keep
            draw.rectangle([10, 8, 22, 28], fill=self.colors['dark_gray'])
            # Towers
            draw.rectangle([6, 10, 10, 24], fill=self.colors['dark_gray'])
            draw.rectangle([22, 10, 26, 24], fill=self.colors['dark_gray'])
            # Crenellations
            for x in range(7, 25, 2):
                draw.rectangle([x, 6, x+1, 8], fill=self.colors['dark_gray'])
            # Gate
            draw.arc([12, 20, 20, 28], 0, 180, fill=self.colors['black'], width=4)
            
        img.save(f"{self.output_dir}/icons/32x32/buildings/{name}.png")
        print(f"‚úÖ Created building: {name}")
        return img

    def generate_all_assets(self):
        """Generate complete asset library"""
        print("üé® Starting comprehensive DVE asset generation...")
        print("=" * 50)
        
        # Status icons
        status_icons = [
            ('ai-success', self.colors['cyber_green'], 'success'),
            ('ai-error', self.colors['crimson'], 'error'),
            ('ai-warning', self.colors['gold'], 'warning'),
            ('ai-thinking', self.colors['purple'], 'thinking'),
            ('ai-sync', self.colors['cyber_green'], 'sync')
        ]
        
        print("üìä Generating status icons...")
        for name, color, pattern in status_icons:
            self.create_status_icon(name, color, pattern)
            
        # Action icons
        action_icons = [
            ('solar-generator', 'solar'),
            ('trading-post', 'trade'),
            ('energy-bolt', 'energy'),
            ('water-pump', 'water'),
            ('food-storage', 'food')
        ]
        
        print("‚öôÔ∏è Generating action icons...")
        for name, icon_type in action_icons:
            self.create_action_icon(name, icon_type)
            
        # Blockchain icons
        blockchain_icons = [
            ('bitcoin', 'bitcoin'),
            ('ethereum', 'ethereum'),
            ('nft-card', 'nft'),
            ('token', 'token'),
            ('smart-contract', 'smart_contract'),
            ('wallet', 'wallet')
        ]
        
        print("‚Çø Generating blockchain icons...")
        for name, blockchain_type in blockchain_icons:
            self.create_blockchain_icon(name, blockchain_type)
            
        # Weapon icons
        weapon_icons = [
            ('assault-rifle', 'rifle'),
            ('pistol', 'pistol'),
            ('sword', 'sword'),
            ('bow', 'bow'),
            ('grenade', 'grenade'),
            ('sniper-rifle', 'sniper')
        ]
        
        print("‚öîÔ∏è Generating weapon icons...")
        for name, weapon_type in weapon_icons:
            self.create_weapon_icon(name, weapon_type)
            
        # Vehicle icons
        vehicle_icons = [
            ('car', 'car'),
            ('truck', 'truck'),
            ('motorcycle', 'motorcycle'),
            ('helicopter', 'helicopter'),
            ('tank', 'tank'),
            ('boat', 'boat')
        ]
        
        print("üöó Generating vehicle icons...")
        for name, vehicle_type in vehicle_icons:
            self.create_vehicle_icon(name, vehicle_type)
            
        # NPC characters
        characters = [
            ('npc-trader', 'trader'),
            ('npc-engineer', 'engineer'),
            ('npc-warrior', 'warrior'),
            ('npc-mage', 'mage')
        ]
        
        print("üë• Generating character sprites...")
        for name, char_type in characters:
            self.create_npc_character(name, char_type)
            
        # Buildings
        buildings = [
            ('solar-farm', 'solar_farm'),
            ('trading-hub', 'trading_post'),
            ('fortress', 'fortress')
        ]
        
        print("üè∞ Generating building sprites...")
        for name, building_type in buildings:
            self.create_building_icon(name, building_type)
            
        print("=" * 50)
        print("üöÄ Comprehensive asset generation complete!")
        print(f"üìÅ All assets saved to: {self.output_dir}")
        print("‚úÖ Ready for integration into DVE system!")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    generator = PixelArtGenerator()
    generator.generate_all_assets()

## üé¨ 2. Complete Sprite Animator (`generators/sprite_animator.py`)

```python
# generators/sprite_animator.py
from PIL import Image, ImageDraw, ImageColor
import numpy as np
import os
import math

class SpriteAnimator:
    def __init__(self, output_dir="dvr-assets/sprites/animated"):
        self.output_dir = output_dir
        os.makedirs(output_dir, exist_ok=True)
        self.colors = {
            'gold': '#FFD700',
            'cyber_green': '#00FF88', 
            'crimson': '#FF4500',
            'purple': '#8A2BE2',
            'blue': '#0080FF',
            'white': '#FFFFFF',
            'black': '#000000',
            'silver': '#C0C0C0'
        }
        
    def create_thinking_animation(self):
        """Create rotating brain thinking animation with enhanced details"""
        frames = []
        colors = ['#8A2BE2', '#9A3BE2', '#AA4BE2', '#BA5BE2', '#CA6BE2', '#DA7BE2', '#EA8BE2', '#FA9BE2']
        
        for i in range(16):  # More frames for smoother animation
            frame = Image.new('RGBA', (32, 32), (0, 0, 0, 0))
            draw = ImageDraw.Draw(frame)
            
            # Rotating brain pattern
            angle = i * 22.5  # 16 frames = 360/16 = 22.5 degrees per frame
            color = colors[i % len(colors)]
            
            # Main brain outline
            draw.ellipse([6, 4, 26, 24], outline=color, width=2)
            
            # Brain hemisphere division
            draw.arc([8, 6, 24, 22], 270, 450, fill=color, width=1)
            
            # Brain details (gyrus patterns)
            draw.arc([10, 8, 22, 16], 0, 180, fill=color, width=1)
            draw.arc([10, 12, 22, 20], 180, 360, fill=color, width=1)
            draw.arc([12, 10, 20, 18], 45, 225, fill=color, width=1)
            
            # Pulsing thought dots around brain
            for j in range(6):
                dot_angle = angle + j * 60
                x = 16 + int(14 * math.cos(math.radians(dot_angle)))
                y = 14 + int(10 * math.sin(math.radians(dot_angle)))
                size = 2 + int(math.sin(math.radians(angle + j * 30)))
                draw.ellipse([x-size, y-size, x+size, y+size], fill=color)
                
            # Central pulse
            pulse_size = 2 + int(math.sin(math.radians(angle * 2)))
            draw.ellipse([16-pulse_size, 14-pulse_size, 16+pulse_size, 14+pulse_size], 
                        fill=color, outline=self.colors['white'])
                
            frames.append(frame)
            
        # Save as GIF
        frames[0].save(f"{self.output_dir}/thinking.gif", 
                      save_all=True, append_images=frames[1:], 
                      duration=150, loop=0)
        print("‚úÖ Created thinking animation")
        
    def create_syncing_animation(self):
        """Create enhanced circular sync animation with multiple layers"""
        frames = []
        
        for i in range(24):  # More frames for ultra-smooth rotation
            frame = Image.new('RGBA', (32, 32), (0, 0, 0, 0))
            draw = ImageDraw.Draw(frame)
            
            # Primary rotation angle
            angle = i * 15  # 24 frames = 360/24 = 15 degrees per frame
            center = (16, 16)
            
            # Outer sync ring
            outer_radius = 12
            for j in range(8):
                arrow_angle = angle + j * 45
                x1 = center[0] + int(outer_radius * math.cos(math.radians(arrow_angle)))
                y1 = center[1] + int(outer_radius * math.sin(math.radians(arrow_angle)))
                x2 = center + int((outer_radius-4) * math.cos(math.radians(arrow_angle+20)))
                y2 = center[1] + int((outer_radius-4) * math.sin(math.radians(arrow_angle+20)))
                
                # Fade based on position
                alpha = int(255 * (0.3 + 0.7 * math.sin(math.radians(arrow_angle - angle))))
                color_with_alpha = (*ImageColor.getrgb(self.colors['cyber_green']), alpha)
                
                draw.line([(x1, y1), (x2, y2)], fill=self.colors['cyber_green'], width=2)
                # Arrow head
                draw.polygon([(x1, y1), (x1-2, y1-2), (x1+2, y1+2)], fill=self.colors['cyber_green'])
                
            # Inner counter-rotating ring
            inner_radius = 8
            inner_angle = -angle * 1.5  # Counter-rotate at different speed
            for j in range(6):
                arrow_angle = inner_angle + j * 60
                x1 = center[0] + int(inner_radius * math.cos(math.radians(arrow_angle)))
                y1 = center[1] + int(inner_radius * math.sin(math.radians(arrow_angle)))
                x2 = center + int((inner_radius-3) * math.cos(math.radians(arrow_angle-15)))
                y2 = center[1] + int((inner_radius-3) * math.sin(math.radians(arrow_angle-15)))
                
                draw.line([(x1, y1), (x2, y2)], fill=self.colors['gold'], width=1)
                
            # Central pulsing core
            pulse_size = 3 + int(2 * math.sin(math.radians(angle * 3)))
            draw.ellipse([center[0]-pulse_size, center[1]-pulse_size, 
                         center+pulse_size, center[1]+pulse_size], 
                        fill=self.colors['white'])
                
            frames.append(frame)
            
        frames.save(f"{self.output_dir}/syncing.gif",
                      save_all=True, append_images=frames[1:],
                      duration=80, loop=0)
        print("‚úÖ Created syncing animation")
                      
    def create_energy_pulse(self):
        """Create complex energy wave pulse animation with multiple effects"""
        frames = []
        
        for i in range(32):  # Longer animation cycle
            frame = Image.new('RGBA', (32, 32), (0, 0, 0, 0))
            draw = ImageDraw.Draw(frame)
            
            # Primary expanding energy rings
            for ring in range(5):
                radius = (i + ring * 6) % 18 + 3
                alpha = max(50, 255 - (i + ring * 6) * 12)
                
                if alpha > 50:
                    # Create color gradient effect
                    if ring % 2 == 0:
                        color = self.colors['cyber_green']
                    else:
                        color = self.colors['blue']
                        
                    # Outer glow
                    draw.ellipse([16-radius-1, 16-radius-1, 16+radius+1, 16+radius+1], 
                               outline=color, width=1)
                    # Main ring
                    draw.ellipse([16-radius, 16-radius, 16+radius, 16+radius], 
                               outline=color, width=2)
                    
            # Lightning-like energy tendrils
            for tendril in range(8):
                tendril_angle = tendril * 45 + i * 5  # Slow rotation
                base_length = 8
                length_variation = int(4 * math.sin(math.radians(i * 10 + tendril * 30)))
                final_length = base_length + length_variation
                
                x1 = 16
                y1 = 16
                x2 = 16 + int(final_length * math.cos(math.radians(tendril_angle)))
                y2 = 16 + int(final_length * math.sin(math.radians(tendril_angle)))
                
                # Add some randomness to make it look like electricity
                mid_x = (x1 + x2) // 2 + int(2 * math.sin(math.radians(i * 20 + tendril * 45)))
                mid_y = (y1 + y2) // 2 + int(2 * math.cos(math.radians(i * 15 + tendril * 60)))
                
                draw.line([(x1, y1), (mid_x, mid_y)], fill=self.colors['white'], width=1)
                draw.line([(mid_x, mid_y), (x2, y2)], fill=self.colors['cyber_green'], width=1)
                
            # Central energy core with pulsing effect
            core_size = 4 + int(3 * math.sin(math.radians(i * 20)))
            draw.ellipse([16-core_size, 16-core_size, 16+core_size, 16+core_size], 
                        fill=self.colors['white'], outline=self.colors['cyber_green'], width=1)
            
            # Inner core
            inner_core = max(1, core_size - 2)
            draw.ellipse([16-inner_core, 16-inner_core, 16+inner_core, 16+inner_core], 
                        fill=self.colors['cyber_green'])
            
            frames.append(frame)
            
        frames[0].save(f"{self.output_dir}/energy_pulse.gif",
                      save_all=True, append_images=frames[1:],
                      duration=60, loop=0)
        print("‚úÖ Created energy pulse animation")

    def create_minting_animation(self):
        """Create NFT minting animation with card flip effect"""
        frames = []
        
        for i in range(20):
            frame = Image.new('RGBA', (32, 32), (0, 0, 0, 0))
            draw = ImageDraw.Draw(frame)
            
            # Card flip effect
            flip_progress = i / 19.0
            card_width = int(16 * abs(math.cos(flip_progress * math.pi)))
            
            if card_width > 0:
                # Card outline
                card_left = 16 - card_width // 2
                card_right = 16 + card_width // 2
                
                if flip_progress  8:
                        draw.text((card_left + 2, 10), "?", fill=self.colors['white'])
                else:
                    # Back of card (after flip) 
                    draw.rectangle([card_left, 6, card_right, 26], 
                                 fill=self.colors['gold'], outline=self.colors['white'], width=1)
                    # NFT content
                    if card_width > 8:
                        draw.rectangle([card_left + 1, 8, card_right - 1, 18], 
                                     fill=self.colors['cyber_green'])
                        draw.text((card_left + 2, 20), "NFT", fill=self.colors['white'])
            
            # Sparkle effects
            for j in range(6):
                sparkle_angle = (i * 30 + j * 60) % 360
                sparkle_radius = 12 + int(2 * math.sin(math.radians(i * 15 + j * 30)))
                x = 16 + int(sparkle_radius * math.cos(math.radians(sparkle_angle)))
                y = 16 + int(sparkle_radius * math.sin(math.radians(sparkle_angle)))
                
                if 0  0.6:
                # Success sparkles
                for j in range(4):
                    sparkle_x = 14 + int(4 * math.cos(math.radians(i * 45 + j * 90)))
                    sparkle_y = 14 + int(4 * math.sin(math.radians(i * 45 + j * 90)))
                    draw.ellipse([sparkle_x, sparkle_y, sparkle_x+2, sparkle_y+2], 
                               fill=self.colors['cyber_green'])
                
                # Success checkmark
                draw.line([(12, 16), (15, 19), (20, 14)], fill=self.colors['cyber_green'], width=2)
            
            frames.append(frame)
            
        frames[0].save(f"{self.output_dir}/trading_success.gif",
                      save_all=True, append_images=frames[1:],
                      duration=120, loop=0)
        print("‚úÖ Created trading success animation")

    def create_error_blink(self):
        """Create error blink animation"""
        frames = []
        
        for i in range(8):
            frame = Image.new('RGBA', (32, 32), (0, 0, 0, 0))
            draw = ImageDraw.Draw(frame)
            
            # Alternating intensity
            if i % 2 == 0:
                color = self.colors['crimson']
                width = 3
            else:
                color = '#AA0000'  # Dimmer red
                width = 2
                
            # Error X
            draw.line([(8, 8), (24, 24)], fill=color, width=width)
            draw.line([(8, 24), (24, 8)], fill=color, width=width)
            
            # Error circle
            draw.ellipse([6, 6, 26, 26], outline=color, width=width)
            
            frames.append(frame)
            
        frames[0].save(f"{self.output_dir}/error_blink.gif",
                      save_all=True, append_images=frames[1:],
                      duration=200, loop=0)
        print("‚úÖ Created error blink animation")

    def create_npc_dialogue_animation(self):
        """Create NPC dialogue animation with talking head"""
        frames = []
        
        for i in range(12):
            frame = Image.new('RGBA', (32, 32), (0, 0, 0, 0))
            draw = ImageDraw.Draw(frame)
            
            # Head
            draw.ellipse([8, 6, 24, 22], fill=self.colors['white'], 
                        outline=self.colors['black'], width=1)
            
            # Eyes
            draw.ellipse([11, 10, 13, 12], fill=self.colors['black'])
            draw.ellipse([19, 10, 21, 12], fill=self.colors['black'])
            
            # Animated mouth (talking effect)
            mouth_frame = i % 4
            if mouth_frame == 0:
                draw.ellipse([14, 16, 18, 18], outline=self.colors['black'], width=1)
            elif mouth_frame == 1:
                draw.ellipse([15, 16, 17, 18], fill=self.colors['black'])
            elif mouth_frame == 2:
                draw.line([(14, 17), (18, 17)], fill=self.colors['black'], width=1)
            else:
                draw.arc([14, 15, 18, 19], 0, 180, fill=self.colors['black'], width=1)
            
            # Speech bubble
            draw.ellipse([20, 4, 30, 12], fill=self.colors['white'], 
                        outline=self.colors['black'], width=1)
            # Speech bubble tail
            draw.polygon([(20, 10), (18, 12), (22, 12)], fill=self.colors['white'], 
                        outline=self.colors['black'])
            
            # Animated dots in speech bubble
            dot_frame = (i // 2) % 3
            for j in range(3):
                dot_x = 22 + j * 2
                dot_y = 8

  const [isVisible, setIsVisible] = useState(false);
  const [currentFrame, setCurrentFrame] = useState(0);
  const [isHovered, setIsHovered] = useState(false);
  const audioRef = useRef(null);
  const responseRef = useRef(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    // Entrance animation
    const timer = setTimeout(() => setIsVisible(true), 100);
    
    // Play sound effect if enabled
    if (enableSound && audioRef.current) {
      audioRef.current.play().catch(() => {
        // Ignore autoplay policy errors
      });
    }

    // Animate thinking/processing states
    if (type === 'thinking' || type === 'processing' || type === 'sync') {
      const interval = setInterval(() => {
        setCurrentFrame(prev => (prev + 1) % 16);
      }, 150);
      return () => {
        clearTimeout(timer);
        clearInterval(interval);
      };
    }

    return () => clearTimeout(timer);
  }, [type, enableSound]);

  // Intersection Observer for scroll animations
  useEffect(() => {
    const observer = new IntersectionObserver(
      ([entry]) => {
        if (entry.isIntersecting) {
          setIsVisible(true);
        }
      },
      { threshold: 0.1 }
    );

    if (responseRef.current) {
      observer.observe(responseRef.current);
    }

    return () => observer.disconnect();
  }, []);

  const getStatusIcon = () => {

      error: '/dvr-assets/icons/16x16/status/ai-error.png', 
      warning: '/dvr-assets/icons/16x16/status/ai-warning.png',
      thinking: '/dvr-assets/sprites/animated/thinking.gif',
      sync: '/dvr-assets/sprites/animated/syncing.gif',
      energy: '/dvr-assets/sprites/animated/energy_pulse.gif',
      minting: '/dvr-assets/sprites/animated/minting.gif',
      trading: '/dvr-assets/sprites/animated/trading_success.gif',
      processing: '/dvr-assets/sprites/animated/thinking.gif',
      dialogue: '/dvr-assets/sprites/animated/npc_dialogue.gif'
    };
    return iconMap[type] || iconMap.thinking;
  };

  const getCharacterAvatar = () => {
    const avatarMap = {
      trader: '/dvr-assets/icons/32x32/characters/npc-trader.png',

      mage: '/dvr-assets/icons/32x32/characters/npc-mage.png'

  const getEmotionIndicator = () => {

      happy: 'üòä',

      money: 'üí∞',
      energy: '‚ö°',
      magic: '‚ú®'
    };
    return emotions[emotion] || emotions.neutral;
  };

  const getContextualIcon = () => {
    if (content.toLowerCase().includes('blockchain') || content.toLowerCase().includes('nft')) {
      return '/dvr-assets/icons/16x16/blockchain/nft-card.png';
    }
    if (content.toLowerCase().includes('weapon') || content.toLowerCase().includes('combat')) {
      return '/dvr-assets/icons/16x16/weapons/sword.png';
    }
    if (content.toLowerCase().includes('vehicle') || content.toLowerCase().includes('transport')) {
      return '/dvr-assets/icons/16x16/vehicles/car.png';
    }
    if (content.toLowerCase().includes('energy') || content.toLowerCase().includes('power')) {
      return '/dvr-assets/icons/16x16/actions/energy-bolt.png';
    }
    if (content.toLowerCase().includes('trade') || content.toLowerCase().includes('sell')) {
      return '/dvr-assets/icons/16x16/actions/trading-post.png';
    }
    return null;
  };

  const getActionButton = () => {
    if (!action) return null;

       {

            action.callback && action.callback();
            onActionClick && onActionClick(action);

  const formatTimestamp = (date) => {
    return new Intl.DateTimeFormat('en-US', {

      second: '2-digit',

    }).format(new Date(date));
  };

  const handleCopy = async () => {
    try {
      await navigator.clipboard.writeText(content);
      // Could add toast notification here
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Failed to copy text:', err);
    }

      try {
        await navigator.share({

          text: content,
          url: window.location.href
        });
      } catch (err) {
        console.error('Failed to share:', err);
      }
    }
  };

EnhancedAIResponse.propTypes = {
  content: PropTypes.string.isRequired,
  type: PropTypes.oneOf([
    'success', 'error', 'warning', 'thinking', 'sync', 'energy', 
    'minting', 'trading', 'processing', 'dialogue', 'default'
  ]),
  status: PropTypes.oneOf(['success', 'error', 'warning', 'info']),
  emotion: PropTypes.oneOf([
    'happy', 'excited', 'concerned', 'success', 'working', 'neutral',
    'thinking', 'celebrating', 'warning', 'error', 'money', 'energy', 'magic'
  ]),
  action: PropTypes.shape({
    label: PropTypes.string.isRequired,
    icon: PropTypes.string,
    callback: PropTypes.func,
    disabled: PropTypes.bool,
    primary: PropTypes.bool,
    tooltip: PropTypes.string,
    badge: PropTypes.string
  }),
  metadata: PropTypes.shape({
    progress: PropTypes.number,
    stats: PropTypes.object,
    resources: PropTypes.object
  }),
  timestamp: PropTypes.oneOfType([PropTypes.string, PropTypes.instanceOf(Date)]),
  characterType: PropTypes.oneOf(['trader', 'engineer', 'warrior', 'mage']),
  enableSound: PropTypes.bool,
  onActionClick: PropTypes.func
};

export default EnhancedAIResponse;
```

```jsx
// Example usage showcasing all the new features
import React from 'react';
import EnhancedAIResponse from './EnhancedAIResponse';

const ExampleUsage = () => {
  return (
    
      {/* Blockchain/NFT Response */}
      Empire Guardian NFT! This unique digital asset represents your status as a founding member of the Virtual Empire. The NFT includes exclusive access to premium trading zones and special governance voting rights."
        type="minting"
        status="success"
        emotion="celebrating"
        characterType="mage"
        action={{
          label: "View NFT",
          icon: "/dvr-assets/icons/16x16/blockchain/nft-card.png",
          callback: () => console.log("Opening NFT viewer..."),
          primary: true,
          tooltip: "Open your new NFT in the gallery",
          badge: "NEW"
        }}
        metadata={{
          stats: {
            "NFT ID": "#4721",
            "Rarity": "Legendary", 
            "Value": "2.5 ETH",
            "Minted": "Just now"
          },
          resources: {
            "ethereum": "2.5 ETH",
            "trading-post": "50 GP"
          }
        }}
        onActionClick={(action) => console.log("Action clicked:", action)}
      />

      {/* Weapon/Combat Response */}
      Combat Analysis Complete!Your assault rifle has been upgraded with advanced targeting systems. Damage output increased by 35% and accuracy improved by 28%. Ready for the next battle, Commander!"
        type="success"
        status="success"
        emotion="excited"
        characterType="warrior"
        action={{
          label: "Test Weapon",
          icon: "/dvr-assets/icons/16x16/weapons/assault-rifle.png",
          callback: () => console.log("Opening weapon testing..."),
          secondary: true,
          tooltip: "Test your upgraded weapon"
        }}
        metadata={{
          stats: {
            "Damage": "+35%",
            "Accuracy": "+28%",
            "Range": "500m",
            "Ammo": "30/120"
          }
        }}
      />

      {/* Vehicle/Transport Response */}
       console.log("Starting convoy..."),
          primary: true,
          tooltip: "Begin the convoy mission"
        }}
        metadata={{
          progress: 85,
          stats: {
            "Vehicles": "4/4 Ready",
            "Fuel": "100%",
            "ETA": "2 hours",
            "Route": "Secure"
          },
          resources: {
            "energy-bolt": "500 Units",
            "trading-post": "1,200 GP"
          }
        }}
      />

      {/* Trading/Economic Response */}
      Trading Post Update: Market conditions are favorable! Your solar energy surplus has attracted premium buyers. Current energy price: 25 GP per unit (‚Üë15% from yesterday). Recommend selling now for maximum profit."
        type="trading"
        status="success"
        emotion="money"
        characterType="trader"
        action={{
          label: "Execute Trade",
          icon: "/dvr-assets/icons/16x16/actions/trading-post.png",
          callback: () => console.log("Executing trade..."),
          primary: true,
          tooltip: "Sell energy at current market rate"
        }}
        metadata={{
          stats: {
            "Energy Stock": "2,400 Units",
            "Current Price": "25 GP/Unit",
            "Potential Profit": "60,000 GP",
            "Market Trend": "‚Üë Bullish"
          }
        }}
      />

      {/* Error with Blockchain Context */}
      Smart Contract Execution Failed: Insufficient gas fees for the transaction. Current network congestion requires 0.025 ETH for successful execution. Please add funds to your wallet and retry."
        type="error"
        status="error"
        emotion="concerned"

## ‚úÖ Complete Integration Ready

MikeLittOrUs, you now have a **comprehensive visual asset system** featuring:

### üé® **Generated Assets**
- **Status Icons**: Success, error, warning, thinking, sync (16x16)
- **Action Icons**: Solar, trading, energy, water, food (16x16) 
- **Blockchain Icons**: Bitcoin, Ethereum, NFT, tokens, smart contracts, wallets (16x16)
- **Weapon Icons**: Rifles, pistols, swords, bows, grenades, sniper rifles (16x16)
- **Vehicle Icons**: Cars, trucks, motorcycles, helicopters, tanks, boats (16x16)
- **Character Sprites**: Trader, engineer, warrior, mage (32x32)
- **Building Sprites**: Solar farms, trading posts, fortresses (32x32)

### üé¨ **Animated Sprites**
- **Thinking Animation**: 16-frame rotating brain with pulsing dots
- **Syncing Animation**: 24-frame dual-ring rotation system
- **Energy Pulse**: 32-frame expanding energy waves with lightning
- **Minting Animation**: 20-frame NFT card flip with sparkles
- **Trading Success**: 16-frame coin exchange with celebration
- **Error Blink**: 8-frame alternating error display
- **NPC Dialogue**: 12-frame talking head with speech bubble

### ‚öõÔ∏è **React Component Features**
- **Dynamic Status**: Success, error, warning, info states
- **Character Types**: Trader, engineer, warrior, mage avatars
- **Emotion System**: 13 different emotional expressions
- **Contextual Icons**: Auto-detects blockchain, weapons, vehicles in text
- **Progress Tracking**: Animated progress bars
- **Resource Display**: Visual resource counters
- **Action Buttons**: Primary/secondary with badges and tooltips
- **Sound Effects**: Audio feedback for different states
- **Responsive Design**: Mobile-optimized layouts
- **Accessibility**: High contrast, reduced motion support

## üéØ 1. Master Deployment Script (`scripts/master/deploy-master.sh`)

```bash
#!/bin/bash
# DVE Master Deployment Script
# Version: 1.0.0
# Author: MikeLittOrUs
# Purpose: Complete DVE system deployment automation

set -euo pipefail

# Configuration
readonly SCRIPT_DIR="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")" && pwd)"
readonly PROJECT_ROOT="$(dirname "$(dirname "$SCRIPT_DIR")")"
readonly LOG_FILE="${PROJECT_ROOT}/logs/deployment-$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S).log"
readonly CONFIG_FILE="${PROJECT_ROOT}/config/master-config.yaml"

# Colors for output
readonly RED='\033[0;31m'
readonly GREEN='\033[0;32m'
readonly YELLOW='\033[1;33m'
readonly BLUE='\033[0;34m'
readonly PURPLE='\033[0;35m'
readonly CYAN='\033[0;36m'
readonly NC='\033[0m' # No Color

# Global variables
DEPLOYMENT_TYPE="development"
SKIP_TESTS=false
FORCE_DEPLOYMENT=false
VERBOSE=false
DRY_RUN=false

# Logging functions
log() {
    local level="$1"
    local message="$2"
    local timestamp=$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')
    echo -e "${timestamp} [${level}] ${message}" | tee -a "$LOG_FILE"
}

info() { log "INFO" "${BLUE}$1${NC}"; }
warn() { log "WARN" "${YELLOW}$1${NC}"; }
error() { log "ERROR" "${RED}$1${NC}"; }
success() { log "SUCCESS" "${GREEN}$1${NC}"; }
debug() { [[ "$VERBOSE" == true ]] && log "DEBUG" "${PURPLE}$1${NC}"; }

# Error handling
cleanup() {
    local exit_code=$?
    if [[ $exit_code -ne 0 ]]; then
        error "Deployment failed with exit code: $exit_code"
        error "Check log file: $LOG_FILE"
        rollback_deployment
    fi
    info "Cleanup completed"
    exit $exit_code
}

trap cleanup EXIT

# Help function
show_help() {
    cat  /dev/null; then
            error "Required command not found: $cmd"
            exit 1
        fi
        debug "‚úì Found: $cmd"
    done
    
    # Check versions
    local node_version=$(node --version | sed 's/v//')
    if ! version_compare "$node_version" "18.0.0"; then
        error "Node.js version $node_version is too old. Minimum required: 18.0.0"
        exit 1
    fi
    
    local python_version=$(python3 --version | awk '{print $2}')
    if ! version_compare "$python_version" "3.9.0"; then
        error "Python version $python_version is too old. Minimum required: 3.9.0"
        exit 1
    fi
    
    debug "System requirements check passed"
}

version_compare() {
    local version1="$1"
    local version2="$2"
    
    if [[ "$(printf '%s\n' "$version2" "$version1" | sort -V | head -n1)" == "$version2" ]]; then
        return 0
    else
        return 1
    fi
}

check_dependencies() {
    info "Checking dependencies..."
    
    # Check Docker
    if ! docker info &> /dev/null; then
        error "Docker is not running"
        exit 1
    fi
    
    # Check Kubernetes
    if [[ "$DEPLOYMENT_TYPE" != "development" ]]; then
        if ! kubectl cluster-info &> /dev/null; then
            error "Kubernetes cluster is not accessible"
            exit 1
        fi
    fi
    
    # Check network connectivity
    if ! curl -s --max-time 5 https://github.com &> /dev/null; then
        error "No internet connectivity"
        exit 1
    fi
    
    debug "Dependencies check passed"
}

check_configuration() {
    info "Checking configuration..."
    
    if [[ ! -f "$CONFIG_FILE" ]]; then
        error "Configuration file not found: $CONFIG_FILE"
        exit 1
    fi
    
    # Validate configuration file
    if ! yq eval '.' "$CONFIG_FILE" &> /dev/null; then
        error "Invalid YAML in configuration file"
        exit 1
    fi
    
    # Check required configuration keys
    local required_keys=(".database.url" ".redis.url" ".blockchain.networks" ".security.jwt_secret")
    for key in "${required_keys[@]}"; do
        if ! yq eval "$key" "$CONFIG_FILE" &> /dev/null; then
            error "Missing configuration key: $key"
            exit 1
        fi
    done
    
    debug "Configuration check passed"
}

check_system_resources() {
    info "Checking system resources..."
    
    # Check disk space (minimum 10GB)
    local available_space=$(df / | awk 'NR==2 {print $4}')
    local required_space=10485760  # 10GB in KB
    
    if [[ $available_space -lt $required_space ]]; then
        error "Insufficient disk space. Required: 10GB, Available: $(($available_space / 1024 / 1024))GB"
        if [[ "$FORCE_DEPLOYMENT" != true ]]; then
            exit 1
        fi
    fi
    
    # Check memory (minimum 4GB)
    local available_memory=$(free | awk '/^Mem:/{print $2}')
    local required_memory=4194304  # 4GB in KB
    
    if [[ $available_memory -lt $required_memory ]]; then
        warn "Low memory detected. Required: 4GB, Available: $(($available_memory / 1024 / 1024))GB"
    fi
    
    debug "System resources check passed"
}

run_security_checks() {
    info "Running security checks..."
    
    # Check for sensitive files
    if [[ -f ".env" ]] && grep -q "password\|secret\|key" .env; then
        warn "Sensitive data detected in .env file"
    fi
    
    # Check file permissions
    find . -name "*.sh" -not -perm 755 -exec chmod 755 {} \;
    
    # Check for hardcoded secrets
    if grep -r "password\|secret\|key.*=" . --include="*.js" --include="*.py" --include="*.go" | grep -v node_modules | grep -v ".git"; then
        warn "Potential hardcoded secrets detected"
    fi
    
    debug "Security checks completed"
}

# Environment setup
setup_environment() {
    info "üõ†Ô∏è  Setting up environment for $DEPLOYMENT_TYPE..."
    
    # Create necessary directories
    create_directories
    
    # Generate configuration files
    generate_configuration
    
    # Setup secrets
    setup_secrets
    
    # Setup databases
    setup_databases
    
    success "‚úÖ Environment setup completed"
}

create_directories() {
    local dirs=(
        "logs"
        "data/postgres"
        "data/redis" 
        "data/assets"
        "config/generated"
        "backups"
        "monitoring"
    )
    
    for dir in "${dirs[@]}"; do
        if [[ "$DRY_RUN" == true ]]; then
            info "Would create directory: $dir"
        else
            mkdir -p "$dir"
            debug "Created directory: $dir"
        fi
    done
}

generate_configuration() {
    info "Generating configuration files..."
    
    if [[ "$DRY_RUN" == true ]]; then
        info "Would generate configuration for: $DEPLOYMENT_TYPE"
        return
    fi
    
    # Generate Docker Compose file
    generate_docker_compose
    
    # Generate Kubernetes manifests
    if [[ "$DEPLOYMENT_TYPE" != "development" ]]; then
        generate_kubernetes_manifests
    fi
    
    # Generate application configs
    generate_app_configs
}

generate_docker_compose() {
    cat > docker-compose.yml << EOF
version: '3.8'

services:
  # PostgreSQL Database
  postgres:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    container_name: dvr-postgres
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: dvr_db
      POSTGRES_USER: \${DB_USER:-dvr_user}
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: \${DB_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - ./data/postgres:/var/lib/postgresql/data
      - ./scripts/sql:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    restart: unless-stopped
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U \${DB_USER:-dvr_user}"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3

  # Redis Cache
  redis:
    image: redis:

[1] https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/66788286/9341d13d-8054-421d-b704-d8709816346c/GithubProgramming.txt# ALN Universal Language Framework - Complete GitHub Repository
