### 2. src/Main/System/Core/kernel.aln

```aln
# ALN-Kernel v9.0.8 - Core System Kernel
# The heart of the ALN Universal Language Framework
# Manages all system-level operations and resource allocation

# üåê *STRICT* & *STICKY* *TRIGGERS* FOR "KERNEL" & "BOOT"
# *FORCE-TRIGGER* COMMANDS: *KERNEL_BOOT*, *SYSTEM_INIT*, *CORE_START*

@KERNEL {
    @VERSION "9.0.8"
    @BUILD "2025.a8::8::8.53.55"
    @COMPLIANCE ["SOC2", "GDPR", "HIPAA", "PCI-DSS", "ISO27001"]
    
    @MEMORY_MANAGER {
        @POOL {
            heap_size: "4GB",
            stack_size: "256MB",
            cache_size: "512MB",
            quantum_buffer: "128MB"
        }
        
        @GARBAGE_COLLECTOR {
            algorithm: "generational",
            frequency: "adaptive",
            threshold: 0.75,
            compaction: true
        }
        
        @ACTION allocate {
            @INPUT {
                size: integer,
                type: string = "heap"
            }
            @EXEC {
                ptr = malloc(size)
                if ptr == null {
                    @THROW "Memory allocation failed"
                }
                register_allocation(ptr, size, type)
                @RETURN ptr
            }
        }
        
        @ACTION deallocate {
            @INPUT {
                ptr: pointer
            }
            @EXEC {
                if is_valid_pointer(ptr) {
                    free(ptr)
                    unregister_allocation(ptr)
                } else {
                    @THROW "Invalid pointer"
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    @PROCESS_MANAGER {
        @SCHEDULER {
            algorithm: "CFS",  # Completely Fair Scheduler
            quantum: "10ms",
            priorities: 40,
            preemptive: true
        }
        
        @ACTION spawn_process {
            @INPUT {
                name: string,
                entry_point: function,
                priority: integer = 20
            }
            @EXEC {
                pid = next_pid()
                process = {
                    "pid": pid,
                    "name": name,
                    "state": "ready",
                    "priority": priority,
                    "entry": entry_point,
                    "resources": {}
                }
                add_to_ready_queue(process)
                @LOG "Process ${name} spawned with PID ${pid}"
                @RETURN pid
            }
        }
        
        @ACTION kill_process {
            @INPUT {
                pid: integer,
                signal: integer = 15  # SIGTERM
            }
            @EXEC {
                process = get_process(pid)
                if process != null {
                    cleanup_resources(process)
                    remove_from_queues(process)
                    @LOG "Process ${pid} terminated"
                } else {
                    @THROW "Process not found"
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    @FILE_SYSTEM {
        @VFS {  # Virtual File System
            mount_points: {},
            root: "/",
            encoding: "UTF-8"
        }
        
        @ACTION mount {
            @INPUT {
                device: string,
                mount_point: string,
                fs_type: string = "ext4"
            }
            @EXEC {
                if !exists(mount_point) {
                    create_directory(mount_point)
                }
                mount_fs(device, mount_point, fs_type)
                @LOG "Mounted ${device} at ${mount_point}"
            }
        }
        
        @ACTION read_file {
            @INPUT {
                path: string,
                encoding: string = "UTF-8"
            }
            @EXEC {
                if !file_exists(path) {
                    @THROW "File not found: ${path}"
                }
                content = read_raw(path)
                decoded = decode(content, encoding)
                @RETURN decoded
            }
        }
        
        @ACTION write_file {
            @INPUT {
                path: string,
                content: string,
                encoding: string = "UTF-8"
            }
            @EXEC {
                encoded = encode(content, encoding)
                write_raw(path, encoded)
                @LOG "File written: ${path}"
            }
        }
    }
    
    @NETWORK_STACK {
        @TCP_IP {
            version: "IPv6",
            fallback: "IPv4",
            ports: range(1, 65535),
            max_connections: 10000
        }
        
        @ACTION listen {
            @INPUT {
                port: integer,
                protocol: string = "tcp"
            }
            @EXEC {
                socket = create_socket(protocol)
                bind(socket, port)
                listen_on(socket)
                @LOG "Listening on port ${port}"
                @RETURN socket
            }
        }
        
        @ACTION connect {
            @INPUT {
                host: string,
                port: integer,
                protocol: string = "tcp"
            }
            @EXEC {
                socket = create_socket(protocol)
                connect_to(socket, host, port)
                @LOG "Connected to ${host}:${port}"
                @RETURN socket
            }
        }
    }
    
    @INTERRUPT_HANDLER {
        @IRQ_TABLE {
            0: "timer",
            1: "keyboard",
            2: "cascade",
            3: "serial_port_2",
            4: "serial_port_1",
            5: "parallel_port_2",
            6: "floppy",
            7: "parallel_port_1",
            8: "rtc",
            9: "acpi",
            10: "available",
            11: "available",
            12: "mouse",
            13: "fpu",
            14: "primary_ata",
            15: "secondary_ata"
        }
        
        @ACTION register_handler {
            @INPUT {
                irq: integer,
                handler: function
            }
            @EXEC {
                if irq < 0 || irq > 15 {
                    @THROW "Invalid IRQ number"
                }
                handlers[irq] = handler
                enable_irq(irq)
                @LOG "Handler registered for IRQ ${irq}"
            }
        }
    }
    
    @BOOTLOADER {
        @ACTION boot {
            @INPUT {
                config_path: string = "/etc/aln/config.json"
            }
            @EXEC {
                @LOG "ALN Kernel v9.0.8 booting..."
                
                # Initialize core subsystems
                init_memory_manager()
                init_process_manager()
                init_file_system()
                init_network_stack()
                init_interrupt_handlers()
                
                # Load configuration
                config = load_config(config_path)
                apply_config(config)
                
                # Start system services
                start_scheduler()
                start_garbage_collector()
                start_network_services()
                
                # Initialize user space
                spawn_init_process()
                
                @LOG "ALN Kernel boot complete"
                @RETURN true
            }
        }
    }
}

# Entry point
@EXEC {
    if [ "$1" == "KERNEL_BOOT" ] || [ "$1" == "SYSTEM_INIT" ] || [ "$1" == "CORE_START" ] {
        @KERNEL.BOOTLOADER.boot()
    } else {
        @LOG "ALN Kernel v9.0.8 - Use KERNEL_BOOT to initialize"
    }
}
```

### 3. src/Main/System/Core/runtime.aln

```aln
# ALN-Runtime v9.0.8 - Runtime Environment Manager
# Manages execution environment, JIT compilation, and optimization

@RUNTIME {
    @VERSION "9.0.8"
    @FEATURES ["JIT", "AOT", "INTERPRETER", "QUANTUM_READY"]
    
    @JIT_COMPILER {
        @CONFIG {
            optimization_level: 3,
            inline_threshold: 100,
            loop_unrolling: true,
            vectorization: true,
            quantum_acceleration: false
        }
        
        @ACTION compile {
            @INPUT {
                source: string,
                target: string = "native"
            }
            @EXEC {
                # Parse source code
                ast = parse(source)
                
                # Semantic analysis
                analyze_semantics(ast)
                
                # Optimization passes
                ast = optimize_dead_code(ast)
                ast = optimize_loops(ast)
                ast = optimize_tail_calls(ast)
                
                # Code generation
                if target == "native" {
                    machine_code = generate_native(ast)
                } elif target == "wasm" {
                    machine_code = generate_wasm(ast)
                } elif target == "quantum" {
                    machine_code = generate_quantum(ast)
                } else {
                    @THROW "Unknown target: ${target}"
                }
                
                @RETURN machine_code
            }
        }
        
        @ACTION hot_patch {
            @INPUT {
                function_name: string,
                new_code: string
            }
            @EXEC {
                # Compile new code
                compiled = compile(new_code)
                
                # Atomic function replacement
                old_ptr = get_function_pointer(function_name)
                new_ptr = load_compiled(compiled)
                
                atomic_swap(old_ptr, new_ptr)
                
                @LOG "Hot patch applied to ${function_name}"
                @RETURN true
            }
        }
    }
    
    @INTERPRETER {
        @STATE {
            stack: [],
            heap: {},
            registers: {},
            pc: 0  # Program counter
        }
        
        @ACTION execute {
            @INPUT {
                bytecode: array<byte>
            }
            @EXEC {
                while pc < bytecode.length {
                    instruction = bytecode[pc]
                    
                    switch instruction {
                        case PUSH: {
                            value = read_operand()
                            stack.push(value)
                        }
                        case POP: {
                            stack.pop()
                        }
                        case ADD: {
                            b = stack.pop()
                            a = stack.pop()
                            stack.push(a + b)
                        }
                        case SUB: {
                            b = stack.pop()
                            a = stack.pop()
                            stack.push(a - b)
                        }
                        case MUL: {
                            b = stack.pop()
                            a = stack.pop()
                            stack.push(a * b)
                        }
                        case DIV: {
                            b = stack.pop()
                            a = stack.pop()
                            if b == 0 {
                                @THROW "Division by zero"
                            }
                            stack.push(a / b)
                        }
                        case JMP: {
                            pc = read_operand()
                            continue
                        }
                        case JZ: {
                            addr = read_operand()
                            if stack.pop() == 0 {
                                pc = addr
                                continue
                            }
                        }
                        case CALL: {
                            addr = read_operand()
                            call_stack.push(pc)
                            pc = addr
                            continue
                        }
                        case RET: {
                            pc = call_stack.pop()
                        }
                        case HALT: {
                            break
                        }
                        default: {
                            @THROW "Unknown instruction: ${instruction}"
                        }
                    }
                    
                    pc++
                }
                
                @RETURN stack.top()
            }
        }
    }
    
    @OPTIMIZER {
        @PROFILER {
            hot_functions: {},
            call_counts: {},
            execution_times: {}
        }
        
        @ACTION profile {
            @INPUT {
                function_name: string
            }
            @EXEC {
                start_time = time_now()
                
                # Execute function with profiling
                result = execute_with_profiling(function_name)
                
                end_time = time_now()
                execution_time = end_time - start_time
                
                # Update statistics
                call_counts[function_name]++
                execution_times[function_name] += execution_time
                
                # Mark as hot if frequently called
                if call_counts[function_name] > 1000 {
                    hot_functions[function_name] = true
                    schedule_optimization(function_name)
                }
                
                @RETURN result
            }
        }
        
        @ACTION optimize {
            @INPUT {
                function_name: string
            }
            @EXEC {
                if !hot_functions[function_name] {
                    @RETURN false
                }
                
                # Get function code
                code = get_function_code(function_name)
                
                # Apply aggressive optimizations
                optimized = apply_optimizations(code, {
                    "inline": true,
                    "unroll_loops": true,
                    "vectorize": true,
                    "eliminate_bounds_checks": true,
                    "specialize_types": true
                })
                
                # JIT compile optimized version
                compiled = JIT_COMPILER.compile(optimized, "native")
                
                # Hot patch the function
                JIT_COMPILER.hot_patch(function_name, compiled)
                
                @LOG "Function ${function_name} optimized"
                @RETURN true
            }
        }
    }
    
    @SANDBOX {
        @PERMISSIONS {
            file_system: "restricted",
            network: "limited",
            memory: "bounded",
            cpu: "throttled"
        }
        
        @ACTION create_sandbox {
            @INPUT {
                config: object
            }
            @EXEC {
                sandbox_id = generate_uuid()
                
                sandbox = {
                    "id": sandbox_id,
                    "memory_limit": config.memory_limit || "256MB",
                    "cpu_quota": config.cpu_quota || 0.5,
                    "allowed_syscalls": config.syscalls || [],
                    "network_access": config.network || false,
                    "filesystem_root": "/sandboxes/${sandbox_id}"
                }
                
                # Create isolated environment
                create_namespace(sandbox_id)
                setup_cgroups(sandbox)
                apply_seccomp_filter(sandbox.allowed_syscalls)
                
                @LOG "Sandbox ${sandbox_id} created"
                @RETURN sandbox_id
            }
        }
        
        @ACTION execute_in_sandbox {
            @INPUT {
                sandbox_id: string,
                code: string
            }
            @EXEC {
                sandbox = get_sandbox(sandbox_id)
                if !sandbox {
                    @THROW "Sandbox not found"
                }
                
                # Switch to sandbox context
                enter_namespace(sandbox_id)
                apply_resource_limits(sandbox)
                
                # Execute code safely
                try {
                    result = INTERPRETER.execute(compile(code))
                } catch (error) {
                    @LOG "Sandbox execution failed: ${error}"
                    @THROW error
                } finally {
                    exit_namespace()
                }
                
                @RETURN result
            }
        }
    }
}
```

### 4. src/Main/System/Security/encryption.aln

```aln
# ALN-Encryption v9.0.8 - Advanced Encryption System
# Quantum-resistant encryption with post-quantum algorithms

@ENCRYPTION {
    @VERSION "9.0.8"
    @ALGORITHMS ["AES-256-GCM", "ChaCha20-Poly1305", "CRYSTALS-Kyber", "SPHINCS+"]
    
    @QUANTUM_RESISTANT {
        @ACTION generate_keypair {
            @INPUT {
                algorithm: string = "CRYSTALS-Kyber",
                security_level: integer = 3  # 1-5, where 5 is highest
            }
            @EXEC {
                if algorithm == "CRYSTALS-Kyber" {
                    # Lattice-based key encapsulation
                    params = get_kyber_params(security_level)
                    private_key = generate_kyber_private(params)
                    public_key = derive_kyber_public(private_key, params)
                } elif algorithm == "SPHINCS+" {
                    # Hash-based signatures
                    params = get_sphincs_params(security_level)
                    private_key = generate_sphincs_private(params)
                    public_key = derive_sphincs_public(private_key, params)
                } else {
                    @THROW "Unknown quantum-resistant algorithm"
                }
                
                @RETURN {
                    "algorithm": algorithm,
                    "public_key": base64_encode(public_key),
                    "private_key": secure_store(private_key),
                    "security_level": security_level
                }
            }
        }
        
        @ACTION encrypt_quantum_safe {
            @INPUT {
                data: string,
                public_key: string
            }
            @EXEC {
                # Hybrid encryption: Classical + Quantum-resistant
                
                # Generate ephemeral symmetric key
                symmetric_key = generate_random_bytes(32)
                
                # Encrypt data with symmetric key (AES-256-GCM)
                iv = generate_random_bytes(12)
                ciphertext = aes_gcm_encrypt(data, symmetric_key, iv)
                
                # Encapsulate symmetric key with quantum-resistant algorithm
                encapsulated = kyber_encapsulate(symmetric_key, public_key)
                
                @RETURN {
                    "ciphertext": base64_encode(ciphertext),
                    "encapsulated_key": base64_encode(encapsulated),
                    "iv": base64_encode(iv),
                    "algorithm": "HYBRID-KYBER-AES"
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    @HOMOMORPHIC {
        @ACTION setup_fhe {
            @INPUT {
                security_parameter: integer = 128
            }
            @EXEC {
                # Setup Fully Homomorphic Encryption
                params = generate_fhe_params(security_parameter)
                keys = generate_fhe_keys(params)
                
                @RETURN {
                    "public_key": keys.public,
                    "evaluation_key": keys.eval,
                    "private_key": secure_store(keys.private)
                }
            }
        }
        
        @ACTION compute_on_encrypted {
            @INPUT {
                encrypted_a: string,
                encrypted_b: string,
                operation: string,
                eval_key: string
            }
            @EXEC {
                # Perform computation on encrypted data
                a = deserialize_ciphertext(encrypted_a)
                b = deserialize_ciphertext(encrypted_b)
                
                if operation == "add" {
                    result = fhe_add(a, b, eval_key)
                } elif operation == "multiply" {
                    result = fhe_multiply(a, b, eval_key)
                } elif operation == "compare" {
                    result = fhe_compare(a, b, eval_key)
                } else {
                    @THROW "Unsupported homomorphic operation"
                }
                
                @RETURN serialize_ciphertext(result)
            }
        }
    }
    
    @KEY_MANAGEMENT {
        @HSM {
            provider: "AWS_CloudHSM",
            cluster_id: "hsm-cluster-1",
            redundancy: 3
        }
        
        @ACTION rotate_keys {
            @INPUT {
                key_id: string,
                grace_period: integer = 86400  # seconds
            }
            @EXEC {
                # Generate new key
                new_key = generate_key()
                new_key_id = store_in_hsm(new_key)
                
                # Mark old key for rotation
                mark_for_rotation(key_id, new_key_id, grace_period)
                
                # Re-encrypt data in background
                schedule_reencryption(key_id, new_key_id)
                
                @LOG "Key rotation scheduled: ${key_id} -> ${new_key_id}"
                @RETURN new_key_id
            }
        }
    }
}
```

```aln
# ALN-Qwen-Integration v9.0.8 - Advanced AI Model Integration
# Integrates Qwen and other AI models for intelligent processing

@QWEN_AI {
    @VERSION "9.0.8"
    @MODELS ["qwen-vl-1.0", "gpt-5", "claude-3", "llama-3"]
    
    @VISION_LANGUAGE {
        @ACTION analyze_image {
            @INPUT {
                image: string,  # base64 encoded
                prompt: string,
                model: string = "qwen-vl-1.0"
            }
            @EXEC {
                # Prepare image for model
                processed_image = preprocess_image(image)
                
                # Create multimodal input
                input_data = {
                    "image": processed_image,
                    "text": prompt,
                    "max_tokens": 2048,
                    "temperature": 0.7
                }
                
                # Call Qwen API
                response = call_qwen_api(input_data, model)
                
                # Post-process response
                analysis = {
                    "description": response.text,
                    "objects": response.detected_objects,
                    "scene": response.scene_understanding,
                    "confidence": response.confidence_score
                }
                
                @RETURN analysis
            }
        }
        
        @ACTION generate_game_assets {
            @INPUT {
                description: string,
                style: string = "pixel-art",
                resolution: string = "32x32"
            }
            @EXEC {
                # Use AI to generate game assets
                prompt = build_asset_prompt(description, style, resolution)
                
                # Generate multiple variations
                variations = []
                for i in range(5) {
                    asset = generate_image(prompt, {
                        "style": style,
                        "resolution": resolution,
                        "seed": random_seed()
                    })
                    variations.append(asset)
                }
                
                # Select best variation
                best_asset = select_best_quality(variations)
                
                @RETURN {
                    "asset": best_asset,
                    "variations": variations,
                    "metadata": {
                        "style": style,
                        "resolution": resolution,
                        "generated_at": timestamp()
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    @NPC_DIALOGUE {
        @ACTION generate_dialogue {
            @INPUT {
                character: object,
                context: string,
                player_input: string,
                faction: string = "neutral"
            }
            @EXEC {
                # Build character context
                character_prompt = build_character_prompt(character, faction)
                
                # Generate contextual response
                response = generate_contextual_response({
                    "system": character_prompt,
                    "context": context,
                    "user": player_input,
                    "max_tokens": 500,
                    "temperature": 0.8
                })
                
                # Apply faction-specific modifications
                response = apply_faction_style(response, faction)
                
                # Ensure dialogue consistency
                response = ensure_consistency(response, character.history)
                
                @RETURN {
                    "dialogue": response,
                    "emotion": detect_emotion(response),
                    "next_options": generate_response_options(response),
                    "faction_reputation_change": calculate_reputation(response, faction)
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    @CODE_GENERATION {
        @ACTION generate_aln_code {
            @INPUT {
                description: string,
                complexity: string = "medium"
            }
            @EXEC {
                # Understand requirements
                requirements = parse_requirements(description)
                
                # Generate ALN code structure
                code_structure = design_architecture(requirements, complexity)
                
                # Generate actual ALN code
                generated_code = generate_code({
                    "language": "ALN",
                    "version": "9.0.8",
                    "requirements": requirements,
                    "structure": code_structure,
                    "style": "idiomatic",
                    "include_comments": true
                })
                
                # Validate generated code
                validation = validate_aln_syntax(generated_code)
                if !validation.valid {
                    generated_code = fix_syntax_errors(generated_code, validation.errors)
                }
                
                # Optimize generated code
                optimized_code = optimize_generated_code(generated_code)
                
                @RETURN {
                    "code": optimized_code,
                    "documentation": generate_docs(optimized_code),
                    "tests": generate_tests(optimized_code),
                    "complexity_score": calculate_complexity(optimized_code)
                }
            }
        }
    }
}
```

### 6. scripts/install.aln

```aln
# ALN-Installer v9.0.8 - Universal Installation Script
# Installs ALN framework on any supported platform

@INSTALLER {
    @VERSION "9.0.8"
    @PLATFORMS ["linux", "macos", "windows", "freebsd", "docker"]
    
    @ACTION install {
        @INPUT {
            prefix: string = "/usr/local",
            features: list<string> = ["core", "developer", "ai", "game-engine"]
        }
        @EXEC {
            @LOG "ALN Universal Language Framework Installer v9.0.8"
            @LOG "================================================"
            
            # Detect platform
            platform = detect_platform()
            @LOG "Detected platform: ${platform}"
            
            # Check prerequisites
            check_prerequisites(platform)
            
            # Download latest release
            @LOG "Downloading ALN v9.0.8..."
            download_url = "https://aln-releases.com/v9.0.8/${platform}/aln.tar.gz"
            download_file(download_url, "/tmp/aln.tar.gz")
            
            # Extract files
            @LOG "Extracting files..."
            extract_archive("/tmp/aln.tar.gz", "/tmp/aln_install")
            
            # Install core components
            @LOG "Installing core components..."
            install_core(prefix)
            
            # Install selected features
            for feature in features {
                @LOG "Installing feature: ${feature}"
                install_feature(feature, prefix)
            }
            
            # Setup environment
            @LOG "Setting up environment..."
            setup_environment(prefix)
            
            # Initialize configuration
            @LOG "Initializing configuration..."
            init_config()
            
            # Run post-install checks
            @LOG "Running post-install checks..."
            if verify_installation(prefix) {
                @LOG "‚úÖ ALN installation completed successfully!"
                @LOG "Run 'aln help' to get started"
            } else {
                @THROW "Installation verification failed"
            }
        }
    }
    
    @ACTION detect_platform {
        @EXEC {
            if (is_linux()) {
                return "linux"
            } elif (is_macos()) {
                return "macos"
            } elif (is_windows()) {
                return "windows"
            } elif (is_freebsd()) {
                return "freebsd"
            } elif (is_docker()) {
                return "docker"
            } else {
                return "unknown"
            }
        }
    }
    
    @ACTION check_prerequisites {
        @INPUT {
            platform: string
        }
        @EXEC {
            required_packages = {
                "linux": ["curl", "wget", "tar", "gzip"],
                "macos": ["curl", "wget", "tar", "gzip"],
                "windows": ["curl", "wget", "tar", "gzip"],
                "freebsd": ["curl", "wget", "tar", "gzip"],
                "docker": ["docker"]
            }
            
            missing_packages = []
            for package in required_packages[platform] {
                if !package_exists(package) {
                    missing_packages.append(package)
                }
            }
            
            if len(missing_packages) > 0 {
                @THROW "Missing required packages: ${missing_packages.join(', ')}"
            }
        }
    }
    
    @ACTION install_core {
        @INPUT {
            prefix: string
        }
        @EXEC {
            # Create installation directories
            mkdir_p("${prefix}/bin")
            mkdir_p("${prefix}/lib")
            mkdir_p("${prefix}/share/aln")
            mkdir_p("${prefix}/etc/aln")
            
            # Copy core binaries
            copy_file("/tmp/aln_install/bin/aln-runtime", "${prefix}/bin/aln-runtime")
            copy_file("/tmp/aln_install/bin/aln-compiler", "${prefix}/bin/aln-compiler")
            copy_file("/tmp/aln_install/bin/aln-cli", "${prefix}/bin/aln-cli")
            
            # Copy libraries
            copy_dir("/tmp/aln_install/lib", "${prefix}/lib")
            
            # Copy shared data
            copy_dir("/tmp/aln_install/share/aln", "${prefix}/share/aln")
            
            # Copy configuration
            copy_file("/tmp/aln_install/etc/aln/config.json", "${prefix}/etc/aln/config.json")
        }
    }
    
    @ACTION install_feature {
        @INPUT {
            feature: string,
            prefix: string
        }
        @EXEC {
            feature_paths = {
                "core": "/tmp/aln_install/features/core",
                "developer": "/tmp/aln_install/features/developer",
                "ai": "/tmp/aln_install/features/ai",
                "game-engine": "/tmp/aln_install/features/game-engine"
            }
            
            if feature in feature_paths {
                copy_dir(feature_paths[feature], "${prefix}/share/aln/features/${feature}")
            } else {
                @THROW "Unknown feature: ${feature}"
            }
        }
    }
    
    @ACTION setup_environment {
        @INPUT {
            prefix: string
        }
        @EXEC {
            # Add to PATH
            shell_profile = get_shell_profile()
            append_to_file(shell_profile, "export PATH=${prefix}/bin:\$PATH")
            
            # Set ALN_HOME
            append_to_file(shell_profile, "export ALN_HOME=${prefix}")
            
            # Create symlinks
            create_symlink("${prefix}/bin/aln-runtime", "/usr/local/bin/aln")
            create_symlink("${prefix}/bin/aln-compiler", "/usr/local/bin/aln-compile")
            create_symlink("${prefix}/bin/aln-cli", "/usr/local/bin/aln-cli")
            
            # Reload shell
            reload_shell()
        }
    }
    
    @ACTION init_config {
        @EXEC {
            # Create default configuration
            config = {
                "runtime": {
                    "version": "9.0.8",
                    "auto_adapt": true,
                    "enable_monitoring": true
                },
                "security": {
                    "enforce_authentication": true,
                    "enable_encryption": true,
                    "key_rotation": "90d"
                },
                "features": {
                    "ai": true,
                    "game_engine": true,
                    "quantum": false
                }
            }
            
            write_file("/etc/aln/config.json", json_encode(config))
        }
    }
    
    @ACTION verify_installation {
        @INPUT {
            prefix: string
        }
        @EXEC {
            # Check if binaries exist
            if !file_exists("${prefix}/bin/aln-runtime") {
                return false
            }
            if !file_exists("${prefix}/bin/aln-compiler") {
                return false
            }
            if !file_exists("${prefix}/bin/aln-cli") {
                return false
            }
            
            # Check if configuration exists
            if !file_exists("/etc/aln/config.json") {
                return false
            }
            
            # Test basic functionality
            try {
                output = run_command("${prefix}/bin/aln-runtime --version")
                if !output.contains("v9.0.8") {
                    return false
                }
            } catch (error) {
                return false
            }
            
            return true
        }
    }
}
```

### 7. scripts/build.aln

```aln
# ALN-Build v9.0.8 - Build System
# Builds ALN framework from source

@BUILDER {
    @VERSION "9.0.8"
    
    @ACTION build {
        @INPUT {
            target: string = "all",
            debug: boolean = false,
            optimize: boolean = true
        }
        @EXEC {
            @LOG "ALN Build System v9.0.8"
            @LOG "========================="
            
            # Set build options
            build_options = {
                "debug": debug,
                "optimize": optimize,
                "target": target
            }
            
            # Initialize build directory
            build_dir = "/tmp/aln-build-${timestamp}"
            mkdir_p(build_dir)
            
            # Build core components
            @LOG "Building core components..."
            build_core_components(build_dir, build_options)
            
            # Build features
            @LOG "Building features..."
            build_features(build_dir, build_options)
            
            # Build documentation
            @LOG "Building documentation..."
            build_documentation(build_dir, build_options)
            
            # Package build
            @LOG "Packaging build..."
            package_build(build_dir, build_options)
            
            @LOG "Build completed successfully!"
            @RETURN {
                "build_directory": build_dir,
                "status": "success",
                "options": build_options
            }
        }
    }
    
    @ACTION build_core_components {

    @ACTION build_features {

            options: object

            @LOG "Building security features..."

            # Build game engine

            # Build modules

    @ACTION build_ai_features {

            build_dir: string,
            options: object
        }

        }
    }
    
    @ACTION build_game_engine {
        @INPUT {
            build_dir: string,
            options: object
        }
        @EXEC {
            # Build game engine
            @LOG "Building game engine..."
            build_game_engine_core(build_dir, options)
            
            # Build game assets
            @LOG "Building game assets..."
            build_game_assets(build_dir, options)
            
            # Build game UI
            @LOG "Building game UI..."
            build_game_ui(build_dir, options)
            
            # Build game logic
            @LOG "Building game logic..."
            build_game_logic(build_dir, options)
        }
    }
    
    @ACTION build_modules {
        @INPUT {
            build_dir: string,
            options: object
        }
        @EXEC {
            # Build blockchain module
            @LOG "Building blockchain module..."
            build_blockchain_module(build_dir, options)
            
            # Build quantum module
            @LOG "Building quantum module..."
            build_quantum_module(build_dir, options)
            
            # Build networking module
            @LOG "Building networking module..."
            build_networking_module(build_dir, options)
        }
    }
    
    @ACTION build_documentation {
        @INPUT {
            build_dir: string,
            options: object
        }
        @EXEC {
            # Generate API documentation
            @LOG "Generating API documentation..."
            generate_api_docs(build_dir, options)
            
            # Generate architecture documentation
            @LOG "Generating architecture documentation..."
            generate_architecture_docs(build_dir, options)
            
            # Generate contributor documentation
            @LOG "Generating contributor documentation..."
            generate_contributor_docs(build_dir, options)
        }
    }
    
    @ACTION package_build {
        @INPUT {
            build_dir: string,
            options: object
        }
        @EXEC {
            # Create package name
            package_name = "aln-framework-v${ALN_VERSION}-${timestamp}.tar.gz"
            package_path = "/tmp/${package_name}"
            
            # Create tarball
            @LOG "Creating package: ${package_path}"
            create_tarball(build_dir, package_path, {
                "exclude": [
                    ".git",
                    "test/",
                    "examples/"
                ]
            })
            
            # Verify package integrity
            @LOG "Verifying package integrity..."
            verify_package(package_path)
            
            @LOG "Package created: ${package_path}"
            @RETURN package_path
        }
    }
}
```

### 8. scripts/deploy.aln

```aln
# ALN-Deploy v9.0.8 - Deployment System
# Deploys ALN framework to various environments

@DEPLOYER {
    @VERSION "9.0.8"
    
    @ENVIRONMENTS {
        "development": {
            "url": "http://dev.aln-system.com",
            "environment": "development",
            "replicas": 1,
            "resources": {
                "cpu": "1",
                "memory": "1Gi"
            },
            "health_check": true
        },
        "staging": {
            "url": "http://staging.aln-system.com",
            "environment": "staging",
            "replicas": 3,
            "resources": {
                "cpu": "2",
                "memory": "2Gi"
            },
            "health_check": true
        },
        "production": {
            "url": "https://aln-system.com",
            "environment": "production",
            "replicas": 5,
            "resources": {
                "cpu": "4",
                "memory": "4Gi"
            },
            "health_check": true,
            "canary_release": true,
            "traffic_shifting": "10% per hour"
        }
    }
    
    @ACTION deploy {
        @INPUT {
            environment: string = "production",
            version: string = "latest",
            rollback: boolean = true,
            health_check: boolean = true
        }
        @EXEC {
            @LOG "ALN Deploy System v9.0.8"
            @LOG "=========================="
            
            # Validate environment
            if !exists(@ENVIRONMENTS[environment]) {
                @THROW "Unknown environment: ${environment}"
            }
            
            # Get environment configuration
            env_config = @ENVIRONMENTS[environment]
            
            # Determine deployment strategy
            if environment == "production" && env_config.canary_release {
                @LOG "Using canary release strategy for production"
                deploy_canary(env_config, version, rollback, health_check)
            } else {
                @LOG "Using standard deployment strategy"
                deploy_standard(env_config, version, rollback, health_check)
            }
            
            @LOG "Deployment completed successfully!"
            @RETURN {
                "environment": environment,
                "version": version,
                "status": "success",
                "deployment_id": generate_uuid()
            }
        }
    }
    
    @ACTION deploy_standard {
        @INPUT {
            env_config: object,
            version: string,
            rollback: boolean,
            health_check: boolean
        }
        @EXEC {
            # Build deployment package
            @LOG "Building deployment package..."
            package_path = build_deployment_package(version)
            
            # Deploy to target environment
            @LOG "Deploying to ${env_config.url}..."
            deploy_to_target(package_path, env_config)
            
            # Apply Kubernetes manifests
            @LOG "Applying Kubernetes manifests..."
            apply_kubernetes_manifests(env_config)
            
            # Wait for deployment to stabilize
            @LOG "Waiting for deployment to stabilize..."
            wait_for_stability(env_config)
            
            # Run health checks
            if health_check {
                @LOG "Running health checks..."
                if !run_health_checks(env_config) {
                    @LOG "Health checks failed"
                    if rollback {
                        @LOG "Rolling back deployment..."
                        rollback_deployment(env_config)
                    } else {
                        @THROW "Health checks failed but rollback disabled"
                    }
                }
            }
            
            @LOG "Standard deployment completed successfully!"
        }
    }
    
    @ACTION deploy_canary {
        @INPUT {
            env_config: object,
            version: string,
            rollback: boolean,
            health_check: boolean
        }
        @EXEC {
            # Build initial canary package
            @LOG "Building initial canary package..."
            canary_version = "${version}-canary"
            canary_package = build_deployment_package(canary_version)
            
            # Deploy canary to 10% of traffic
            @LOG "Deploying canary to 10% of traffic..."
            deploy_canary_traffic(canary_package, env_config, "10%")
            
            # Wait for canary to stabilize
            @LOG "Waiting for canary to stabilize..."
            wait_for_stability(env_config, "10%")
            
            # Run health checks on canary
            if health_check {
                @LOG "Running health checks on canary..."
                if !run_health_checks(env_config, "10%") {
                    @LOG "Canary health checks failed"
                    if rollback {
                        @LOG "Rolling back canary deployment..."
                        rollback_deployment(env_config, "10%")
                    } else {
                        @THROW "Canary health checks failed but rollback disabled"
                    }
                }
            }
            
            # Gradually increase traffic
            @LOG "Gradually increasing traffic..."
            for percentage in [20, 30, 40, 50, 60, 70, 80, 90, 100] {
                @LOG "Increasing traffic to ${percentage}%..."
                update_canary_traffic(env_config, percentage)
                wait_for_stability(env_config, "${percentage}%")
                
                if health_check {
                    @LOG "Running health checks at ${percentage}%..."
                    if !run_health_checks(env_config, "${percentage}%") {
                        @LOG "Health checks failed at ${percentage}%"
                        if rollback {
                            @LOG "Rolling back to previous version..."
                            rollback_deployment(env_config)
                        } else {
                            @THROW "Health checks failed at ${percentage}% but rollback disabled"
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            
            @LOG "Canary release completed successfully!"
        }
    }
    
    @ACTION build_deployment_package {
        @INPUT {
            version: string
        }
        @EXEC {
            # Create build directory
            build_dir = "/tmp/aln-deploy-${timestamp}"
            mkdir_p(build_dir)
            
            # Copy necessary files
            copy_file("src/Main/System/Core/kernel.aln", "${build_dir}/kernel.aln")
            copy_file("src/Main/System/Core/runtime.aln", "${build_dir}/runtime.aln")
            copy_file("src/Main/System/Security/encryption.aln", "${build_dir}/encryption.aln")
            copy_file("src/Main/System/AI/qwen_integration.aln", "${build_dir}/qwen_integration.aln")
            copy_file("scripts/install.aln", "${build_dir}/install.aln")
            copy_file("scripts/build.aln", "${build_dir}/build.aln")
            copy_file("scripts/deploy.aln", "${build_dir}/deploy.aln")
            copy_file("config/default.aln", "${build_dir}/config/default.aln")
            copy_file("config/development.aln", "${build_dir}/config/development.aln")
            copy_file("config/production.aln", "${build_dir}/config/production.aln")
            
            # Create package
            package_name = "aln-deploy-${version}-${timestamp}.tar.gz"
            package_path = "/tmp/${package_name}"
            create_tarball(build_dir, package_path, {
                "exclude": [
                    ".git",
                    "test/",
                    "examples/"
                ]
            })
            
            @LOG "Deployment package created: ${package_path}"
            @RETURN package_path
        }
    }
    
    @ACTION deploy_to_target {
        @INPUT {
            package_path: string,
            env_config: object
        }
        @EXEC {
            # Extract package
            @LOG "Extracting package..."
            extract_archive(package_path, "/tmp/aln-deploy-extracted")
            
            # Copy files to target
            @LOG "Copying files to target..."
            copy_dir("/tmp/aln-deploy-extracted", "/opt/aln")
            
            # Restart service
            @LOG "Restarting ALN service..."
            restart_service()
        }
    }
    
    @ACTION apply_kubernetes_manifests {
        @INPUT {
            env_config: object
        }
        @EXEC {
            # Create namespace
            @LOG "Creating namespace..."
            create_namespace(env_config.environment)
            
            # Apply deployment manifest
            @LOG "Applying deployment manifest..."
            apply_manifest("k8s/deployment.yaml", {
                "replicas": env_config.replicas,
                "image": "aln-framework:${ALN_VERSION}",
                "cpu": env_config.resources.cpu,
                "memory": env_config.resources.memory
            })
            
            # Apply service manifest
            @LOG "Applying service manifest..."
            apply_manifest("k8s/service.yaml", {
                "type": "LoadBalancer"
            })
            
            # Apply ingress manifest
            @LOG "Applying ingress manifest..."
            apply_manifest("k8s/ingress.yaml", {
                "host": env_config.url
            })
        }
    }
    
    @ACTION wait_for_stability {
        @INPUT {
            env_config: object,
            percentage: string = "100%"
        }
        @EXEC {
            # Wait for pods to be ready
            @LOG "Waiting for pods to be ready..."
            wait_for_pods_ready(env_config.replicas)
            
            # Wait for service to be available
            @LOG "Waiting for service to be available..."
            wait_for_service_available()
            
            # Wait for health checks to pass
            if env_config.health_check {
                @LOG "Waiting for health checks to pass..."
                wait_for_health_checks()
            }
            
            @LOG "Stability achieved at ${percentage}"
        }
    }
    
    @ACTION run_health_checks {
        @INPUT {
            env_config: object,
            percentage: string = "100%"
        }
        @EXEC {
            # Run health checks
            @LOG "Running health checks..."
            checks_passed = true
            
            # Check pod status
            pod_status = get_pod_status()
            if pod_status != "Running" {
                @LOG "Pod status: ${pod_status}"
                checks_passed = false
            }
            
            # Check service status
            service_status = get_service_status()
            if service_status != "Active" {
                @LOG "Service status: ${service_status}"
                checks_passed = false
            }
            
            # Check application health
            app_health = get_application_health()
            if app_health != "Healthy" {
                @LOG "Application health: ${app_health}"
                checks_passed = false
            }
            
            # Check metrics
            metrics = get_metrics()
            if metrics.response_time > 500 {
                @LOG "Response time: ${metrics.response_time}ms"
                checks_passed = false
            }
            if metrics.error_rate > 0.01 {
                @LOG "Error rate: ${metrics.error_rate}"
                checks_passed = false
            }
            
            if checks_passed {
                @LOG "All health checks passed"
            } else {
                @LOG "Health checks failed"
            }
            
            @RETURN checks_passed
        }
    }
    
    @ACTION rollback_deployment {
        @INPUT {
            env_config: object,
            percentage: string = "100%"
        }
        @EXEC {
            # Rollback to previous version
            @LOG "Rolling back deployment..."
            rollback_to_previous_version()
            
            # Wait for rollback to complete
            @LOG "Waiting for rollback to complete..."
            wait_for_rollback_complete()
            
            @LOG "Rollback completed successfully"
        }
    }
    
    @ACTION update_canary_traffic {
        @INPUT {
            env_config: object,
            percentage: integer
        }
        @EXEC {
            # Update traffic routing
            @LOG "Updating canary traffic to ${percentage}%..."
            update_traffic_routing(percentage)
            
            # Wait for changes to propagate
            @LOG "Waiting for traffic changes to propagate..."
            wait_for_traffic_propagation()
        }
    }
}
```

### 9. .github/workflows/ci.aln

```aln
# CI Workflow for ALN Universal Language Framework
# Continuous Integration pipeline for ALN

@CI_WORKFLOW {
    @NAME "ALN CI"
    @ON {
        push: {
            branches: ["main", "develop"]
        }
        pull_request: {
            branches: ["main"]
        }
    }
    
    @JOBS {
        @JOB "test" {
            @RUNS_ON "ubuntu-latest"
            @STEPS {
                @STEP "Checkout repository" {
                    @USES "actions/checkout@v4"
                }
                @STEP "Setup ALN" {
                    @RUN "curl -sSL https://aln-releases.com/install.sh | bash"
                    @RUN "echo '$HOME/.aln/bin' >> $GITHUB_PATH"
                }
                @STEP "Install dependencies" {
                    @RUN "pip install -r requirements.txt"
                }
                @STEP "Run tests" {
                    @RUN "aln test --coverage"
                }
                @STEP "Check code quality" {
                    @RUN "aln lint"
                }
                @STEP "Generate coverage report" {
                    @RUN "aln coverage report"
                }
            }
        }
        @JOB "build" {
            @RUNS_ON "ubuntu-latest"
            @STEPS {
                @STEP "Checkout repository" {
                    @USES "actions/checkout@v4"
                }
                @STEP "Setup ALN" {
                    @RUN "curl -sSL https://aln-releases.com/install.sh | bash"
                    @RUN "echo '$HOME/.aln/bin' >> $GITHUB_PATH"
                }
                @STEP "Build ALN framework" {
                    @RUN "aln build --target all"
                }
                @STEP "Upload build artifacts" {
                    @RUN "aln build --upload"
                }
            }
        }
        @JOB "security" {
            @RUNS_ON "ubuntu-latest"
            @STEPS {
                @STEP "Checkout repository" {
                    @USES "actions/checkout@v4"
                }
                @STEP "Setup ALN" {
                    @RUN "curl -sSL https://aln-releases.com/install.sh | bash"
                    @RUN "echo '$HOME/.aln/bin' >> $GITHUB_PATH"
                }
                @STEP "Scan for vulnerabilities" {
                    @RUN "aln scan --vulnerabilities"
                }
                @STEP "Check compliance" {
                    @RUN "aln check --compliance"
                }
                @STEP "Audit for privacy issues" {
                    @RUN "aln audit --privacy"
                }
                @STEP "Check for secrets" {
                    @RUN "gitleaks --source=."
                }
            }
        }
    }
}
```

```aln
# Deployment Workflow for ALN Universal Language Framework
# Automated deployment pipeline for ALN

@DEPLOYMENT_WORKFLOW {
    @NAME "ALN Deployment"
    @ON {
        push: {
            branches: ["main"]
        }
    }
    
    @JOBS {
        @JOB "deploy-production" {
            @RUNS_ON "ubuntu-latest"
            @IF {
                condition: "github.ref == 'refs/heads/main'"
            }
            @STEPS {
                @STEP "Checkout repository" {
                    @USES "actions/checkout@v4"
                }
                @STEP "Setup ALN" {
                    @RUN "curl -sSL https://aln-releases.com/install.sh | bash"
                    @RUN "echo '$HOME/.aln/bin' >> $GITHUB_PATH"
                }
                @STEP "Build ALN framework" {
                    @RUN "aln build --target all"
                }
                @STEP "Deploy to production" {
                    @RUN "aln deploy --env production --canary-release"
                }
                @STEP "Verify deployment" {
                    @RUN "aln verify --env production"
                }
                @STEP "Notify team" {
                    @RUN "aln notify --message 'Production deployment completed successfully'"
                }
            }
        }
        @JOB "deploy-staging" {
            @RUNS_ON "ubuntu-latest"
            @IF {
                condition: "github.ref == 'refs/heads/develop'"
            }
            @STEPS {
                @STEP "Checkout repository" {
                    @USES "actions/checkout@v4"
                }
                @STEP "Setup ALN" {
                    @RUN "curl -sSL https://aln-releases.com/install.sh | bash"
                    @RUN "echo '$HOME/.aln/bin' >> $GITHUB_PATH"
                }
                @STEP "Build ALN framework" {
                    @RUN "aln build --target all"
                }
                @STEP "Deploy to staging" {
                    @RUN "aln deploy --env staging"
                }
                @STEP "Verify deployment" {
                    @RUN "aln verify --env staging"
                }
                @STEP "Notify team" {
                    @RUN "aln notify --message 'Staging deployment completed successfully'"
                }
            }
        }
    }
```

### 14. docs/API.md

```markdown
# ALN Universal Language Framework - API Reference

## Table of Contents
1. [Core System](#core-system)
2. [Security](#security)
3. [AI Integration](#ai-integration)
4. [Game Engine](#game-engine)
5. [Deployment](#deployment)

## Core System

### `@KERNEL`
The core system kernel manages all system-level operations and resource allocation.

#### Methods
- `@ACTION boot`: Initializes the ALN kernel
- `@ACTION shutdown`: Shuts down the ALN system
- `@ACTION restart`: Restarts the ALN system

#### Properties
- `@VERSION`: Current version of the kernel
- `@BUILD`: Build timestamp
- `@COMPLIANCE`: List of compliance standards

### `@RUNTIME`
Manages the execution environment, JIT compilation, and optimization.

#### Methods
- `@ACTION compile`: Compiles ALN code to machine code
- `@ACTION execute`: Executes compiled code
- `@ACTION hot_patch`: Applies hot patches without restarting

#### Properties
- `@VERSION`: Current version of the runtime
- `@FEATURES`: List of enabled features
- `@JIT_COMPILER`: JIT compiler configuration

## Security

### `@ENCRYPTION`
Advanced encryption system with quantum-resistant algorithms.

#### Methods
- `@ACTION generate_keypair`: Generates a public-private key pair
- `@ACTION encrypt_quantum_safe`: Encrypts data using hybrid encryption
- `@ACTION decrypt_quantum_safe`: Decrypts data using hybrid decryption

#### Properties
- `@VERSION`: Current version of the encryption system
- `@ALGORITHMS`: List of supported algorithms
- `@QUANTUM_RESISTANT`: Quantum-resistant encryption configuration

### `@AUTHENTICATION`
Handles user authentication and authorization.

#### Methods
- `@ACTION login`: Authenticates a user
- `@ACTION logout`: Logs out a user
- `@ACTION verify_token`: Verifies a JWT token

#### Properties
- `@VERSION`: Current version of the authentication system
- `@METHODS`: List of supported authentication methods
- `@MFA_REQUIRED`: Whether multi-factor authentication is required

## AI Integration

### `@QWEN_AI`
Integrates Qwen and other AI models for intelligent processing.

#### Methods
- `@ACTION analyze_image`: Analyzes an image using the vision-language model
- `@ACTION generate_game_assets`: Generates game assets based on descriptions
- `@ACTION generate_dialogue`: Generates NPC dialogue with emotional context

#### Properties
- `@VERSION`: Current version of the AI system
- `@MODELS`: List of supported models
- `@VISION_LANGUAGE`: Vision-language model configuration

### `@RAG_SYSTEM`
Retrieval-Augmented Generation system for enhanced knowledge retrieval.

#### Methods
- `@ACTION query`: Queries the knowledge base using vector similarity
- `@ACTION index_document`: Adds a document to the knowledge base
- `@ACTION remove_document`: Removes a document from the knowledge base

#### Properties
- `@VERSION`: Current version of the RAG system
- `@INDEX`: Index configuration
- `@QUERY`: Query configuration

## Game Engine

### `@GAME_ENGINE`
Built-in game engine with pixel-art support.

#### Methods
- `@ACTION create_game`: Creates a new game instance
- `@ACTION start_game`: Starts a game
- `@ACTION stop_game`: Stops a game
- `@ACTION generate_asset`: Generates game assets using AI

#### Properties
- `@VERSION`: Current version of the game engine
- `@STYLE`: Default art style
- `@RESOLUTION`: Default resolution

## Deployment

### `@DEPLOYER`
Deploys ALN framework to various environments.

#### Methods
- `@ACTION deploy`: Deploys to a specified environment
- `@ACTION rollback`: Rolls back a deployment
- `@ACTION verify`: Verifies a deployment

#### Properties
- `@VERSION`: Current version of the deployer
- `@ENVIRONMENTS`: List of supported environments
- `@STRATEGIES`: Deployment strategies
```

```markdown
# ALN Universal Language Framework - Architecture Overview

## Overview

The ALN Universal Language Framework is a revolutionary self-evolving programming language that combines AI integration, quantum computing readiness, and zero-downtime hot patching capabilities. The architecture is designed to be modular, scalable, and highly adaptable to different environments.

## System Architecture

### Layered Architecture
```
+-----------------------------+
|        User Interface       |
+-----------------------------+
|        Application Layer    |
+-----------------------------+
|        Runtime Layer        |
+-----------------------------+
|        Core System Layer    |
+-----------------------------+
|        Hardware Abstraction |
+-----------------------------+
```

### Component Diagram
```
+-------------------------------+
|      ALN Universal Framework  |
+-------------------------------+

|  |  - Kubernetes Integration|  |
|  |  - Canary Releases      |  |
|  +-------------------------+  |
|                               |
+-------------------------------+
```

## Core Components

### 1. Kernel
The kernel is the heart of the ALN Universal Language Framework. It manages all system-level operations and resource allocation.

- **Memory Management**: Handles memory allocation, garbage collection, and memory protection
- **Process Management**: Manages process creation, scheduling, and termination
- **File System**: Provides virtual file system with support for multiple storage backends
- **Network Stack**: Implements TCP/IP stack with IPv6 support
- **Interrupt Handler**: Manages hardware interrupts and system calls

### 2. Runtime
The runtime manages the execution environment, JIT compilation, and optimization.

- **JIT Compiler**: Compiles ALN code to machine code at runtime
- **Interpreter**: Executes compiled code in a sandboxed environment
- **Optimizer**: Profiles code and applies optimizations based on usage patterns
- **Sandbox**: Provides isolated execution environment with resource limits

### 3. Security Module
The security module provides enterprise-grade security features.

- **Encryption**: Quantum-resistant encryption with hybrid algorithms
- **Authentication**: Multi-factor authentication with JWT tokens
- **Compliance**: Built-in compliance with SOC2, GDPR, HIPAA, and PCI-DSS

### 4. AI Integration
The AI integration provides advanced artificial intelligence capabilities.

- **Vision-Language Model**: Analyzes images and generates descriptions
- **RAG System**: Retrieves information from knowledge bases using vector similarity
- **Agent Orchestrator**: Coordinates multiple AI agents for complex tasks

### 5. Game Engine
The game engine provides built-in support for game development.

- **Pixel Art Support**: Native support for pixel art graphics
- **Asset Generation**: Uses AI to generate game assets
- **Game Logic**: Provides tools for creating game mechanics and rules

### 6. Deployment Module
The deployment module handles automated deployment to various environments.

- **CI/CD Pipeline**: Integrates with GitHub Actions for continuous integration
- **Kubernetes Integration**: Deploys to Kubernetes clusters with auto-scaling
- **Canary Releases**: Supports gradual rollouts with traffic shifting

## Data Flow

1. **User Input**: User interacts with the system through the user interface
2. **Request Processing**: Requests are routed to the appropriate component
3. **Execution**: Code is compiled and executed in the runtime environment
4. **Data Storage**: Results are stored in the file system or database
5. **Output Generation**: Results are formatted and returned to the user

## Scalability

The ALN Universal Language Framework is designed to scale horizontally across multiple nodes. The architecture supports:

- **Distributed Computing**: Multiple instances can work together
- **Load Balancing**: Requests are distributed across available nodes
- **Auto-Scaling**: Nodes can be automatically added or removed based on load

## Extensibility

The framework is highly extensible through plugins and custom components. Developers can:

- **Create Custom Plugins**: Extend functionality with new components
- **Modify Existing Components**: Customize behavior of existing modules
- **Integrate with External Systems**: Connect to external APIs and services

## Summary

The ALN Universal Language Framework's layered architecture provides a robust foundation for building complex applications. The modular design allows for easy maintenance and extension, while the focus on security, performance, and scalability ensures reliable operation in production environments.
```

```aln
# Game Example for ALN Universal Language Framework
# This example demonstrates game development capabilities

@GAME_EXAMPLE {
    @TITLE "Simple Game Example"
    @DESCRIPTION "A basic game demonstrating ALN's game engine capabilities"
    
    @ACTION create_game {
        @LOG "Creating a new game..."
        
        # Define game properties
        game = {
            "title": "ALN Adventure",
            "version": "1.0.0",
            "author": "ALN Community",
            "genre": "Adventure",
            "resolution": "320x240",
            "fps": 60,
            "art_style": "pixel-art"
        }
        
        @LOG "Game created: ${game.title}"
        @LOG "Resolution: ${game.resolution}"
        @LOG "Art style: ${game.art_style}"
        
        # Generate game assets
        @LOG "Generating game assets..."
        assets = generate_game_assets({
            "description": "A pixel-art character with sword and shield",
            "style": "pixel-art",
            "resolution": "32x32"
        })
        
        @LOG "Generated ${assets.variations.length} asset variations"
        
        # Create game world
        @LOG "Creating game world..."
        world = {
            "name": "Alnia",
            "size": "100x100",
            "biomes": ["forest", "desert", "mountain"],
            "entities": []
        }
        
        @LOG "Game world created: ${world.name}"
        @LOG "Biomes: ${world.biomes.join(', ')}"
        
        # Create game characters
        @LOG "Creating game characters..."
        characters = []
        
        # Create player character
        player = {
            "name": "Hero",
            "type": "player",
            "health": 100,
            "attack": 20,
            "defense": 15,
            "inventory": [],
            "position": {"x": 50, "y": 50}
        }
        characters.append(player)
        
        # Create enemy character
        enemy = {
            "name": "Goblin",
            "type": "enemy",
            "health": 50,
            "attack": 15,
            "defense": 10,
            "inventory": [{"item": "potion", "quantity": 2}],
            "position": {"x": 75, "y": 75}
        }
        characters.append(enemy)
        
        @LOG "Created ${characters.length} characters"
        
        # Create game state
        @LOG "Creating game state..."
        state = {
            "game": game,
            "world": world,
            "characters": characters,
            "time": "day",
            "weather": "clear",
            "score": 0,
            "level": 1
        }
        
        @LOG "Game state initialized"
        
        @RETURN state
    }
}
```

### 19. examples/ai_chat.aln

```aln
# AI Chat Example for ALN Universal Language Framework
# This example demonstrates AI integration capabilities

@AI_CHAT_EXAMPLE {
    @TITLE "AI Chat Integration"
    @DESCRIPTION "A chat interface demonstrating ALN's AI capabilities"
    
    @ACTION start_chat {
        @LOG "Starting AI chat session..."
        
        # Initialize chat session
        session = {
            "id": generate_uuid(),
            "started_at": timestamp(),
            "model": "qwen-vl-1.0",
            "temperature": 0.7,
            "max_tokens": 2048,
            "history": []
        }
        
        @LOG "Chat session started: ${session.id}"
        @LOG "Model: ${session.model}"
        @LOG "Temperature: ${session.temperature}"
        
        # Welcome message
        @LOG "Welcome to the ALN AI Chat!"
        @LOG "How can I assist you today?"
        
        # Interactive chat loop
        while true {
            # Get user input
            @LOG ""
            @LOG "User: "
            user_input = get_user_input()
            
            # Exit condition
            if user_input.lower() == "exit" || user_input.lower() == "quit" {
                @LOG "Goodbye!"
                break
            }
            
            # Add user message to history
            session.history.append({
                "role": "user",
                "content": user_input,
                "timestamp": timestamp()
            })
            
            # Generate AI response
            @LOG "AI: "
            ai_response = generate_ai_response({
                "messages": session.history,
                "model": session.model,
                "temperature": session.temperature,
                "max_tokens": session.max_tokens
            })
            
            # Add AI message to history
            session.history.append({
                "role": "assistant",
                "content": ai_response,
                "timestamp": timestamp()
            })
            
            # Display AI response
            @LOG ai_response
            
            # Optional: Generate image based on text
            if contains(ai_response, "image") || contains(ai_response, "picture") {
                @LOG ""
                @LOG "Generating image based on the conversation..."
                image_prompt = build_image_prompt(ai_response)
                image_result = analyze_image({
                    "image": image_prompt,
                    "prompt": "Generate a visual representation of the scene described in the text",
                    "model": "qwen-vl-1.0"
                })
                
                @LOG "Image generated: ${image_result.description}"
            }
        }
        
        @LOG "Chat session ended"
        @RETURN session
    }
    
    @FUNCTION build_image_prompt {
        @INPUT {
            text: string
        }
        @EXEC {
            # Extract key elements from text
            keywords = extract_keywords(text)
            
            # Build prompt
            prompt = "A detailed illustration of: " + join(keywords, ", ")
            
            @RETURN prompt
        }
    }
    
    @FUNCTION extract_keywords {
        @INPUT {
            text: string
        }
        @EXEC {
            # Simple keyword extraction
            words = text.split(" ")
            keywords = []
            
            for word in words {
                if length(word) > 3 && !contains(word, "the") && !contains(word, "and") {
                    keywords.append(word.lower())
                }
            }
            
            @RETURN unique(keywords)
        }
    }
}
```

    *   **@RESPONSE_GENERATOR:** Creates contextual responses based on user intent, confidence levels, and available suggestions.
    *   **@SMART_COMMAND_SUGGESTIONS:** Provides intelligent, context-aware command recommendations based on the user's skill level and current task.

### USER


### ASSISTANT
I've analyzed the second uploaded file, `Pasted_Text_1754876403822.txt`. This document details the **core security architecture and operational modes** of the ALN Dev Shell, building upon the command definitions found in the first file.

The key concepts are:

### 1. **Zero-Trust Security Architecture (Core Principle)**
The system operates on a strict "zero-trust" model where **all inputs are automatically sanitized before any function executes**. This is enforced at two levels:
*   **Global Input Sanitization:** The `@INPUT_SANITIZER` block uses a regex (`^[a-zA-Z0-9_\\-\\.\\s]{1,256}$`) to allow only safe characters and explicitly blocks dangerous patterns like `<script>`, `javascript:`, `eval`, `system`, and shell operators (`;`, `&&`, `||`). Inputs are capped at 256 characters.
*   **Function-Level Enforcement:** Every function call is wrapped in a `@SANDBOXED_EXECUTOR` that runs commands in a confined environment with restricted capabilities.

### 2. **Three Operational Modes (Security Contexts)**
The system provides different levels of access based on user intent and risk tolerance:

*   **Sandboxed Mode (Default):**
    *   **Purpose:** Safe execution for routine tasks.
    *   **Features:** Only allows a predefined set of safe operations (`ls`, `pwd`, `cat`, `mkdir`, `touch`, `rm`). Blocks network access (`curl`, `wget`, `ping`, `ssh`) and restricts filesystem access to the `/v://System/ALN/src/Main` directory tree.
    *   **Example:** `aln.terminal.run ls -la /v://System/ALN/src/Main`

*   **Privileged Mode (`--priv`):**
    *   **Purpose:** Execute powerful system commands with explicit user consent.
    *   **Features:** Grants full access to the OS shell, including network tools and file manipulation outside the sandbox.
    *   **Security:** Before executing any potentially dangerous command, the system performs a real-time compliance check against major standards like `PCI_DSS_v4.0` and `NIST_SP_800-53`.
    *   **Example:** `aln.terminal.run --priv curl -s https://api.github.com/repos/ALN-Legal-Systems/legal-ownership-transfer-v1 | grep "commit"`

*   **Root Mode (`--root`):**
    *   **Purpose:** Full administrative control for critical system maintenance.
    *   **Features:** Provides complete system access and control, intended for use only by authorized administrators.

### 3. **Additional Security & System Features**

```aln
// Secure Environment Variables Management
@FUNCTION manage_env_vars {
    description: "Manage sensitive environment variables with encryption and automatic rotation.",
    input: { action: string, key: string, value: string },
    output: { success: bool, message: string }
}

@EXEC {
    if input.action == "set" {
        @ENV_VARS[input.key] = encrypt(input.value)
        @ROTATE_KEYS.rotate()
    } else if input.action == "get" {
        @RETURN { success: true, value: decrypt(@ENV_VARS[input.key]) }
    } else if input.action == "delete" {
        @ENV_VARS.delete(input.key)
        @ROTATE_KEYS.rotate()
    }
    @RETURN { success: true, message: "Environment variable ${input.action}: ${input.key}" }
}
```
